in &#39;buy&#39;">b</span><span title="/\xc9\x9b/: &#39;e&#39; in &#39;dress&#39;">\xc9\x9b</span><span title="&#39;k&#39; in &#39;kind&#39;">k</span><span title="/\xc9\x99m/: &#39;m&#39; in &#39;rhythm&#39;">\xc9\x99m</span></span>/</a></span></span>; born 2 May 1975) is an English retired professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> and current President of <a href="/wiki/Inter_Miami_CF" title="Inter Miami CF">Inter Miami CF</a>. He played for <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>, <a href="/wiki/Preston_North_End_F.C." title="Preston North End F.C.">Preston North End</a>, <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>, <a href="/wiki/LA_Galaxy" title="LA Galaxy">LA Galaxy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> and the <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England national team</a>, for which he held the appearance record for an <a href="/wiki/Outfield#Association_football" title="Outfield">outfield player</a> until 2016. He is the first English player to win league titles in four countries: England, Spain, the United States and France. He retired in May 2013 after a 20-year career, during which he won 19 major trophies.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Known for his range of passing, <a href="/wiki/Cross_(football)" title="Cross (football)">crossing ability</a> and <a href="/wiki/Curl_(football)" title="Curl (football)">bending</a> <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" title="Direct free kick">free-kicks</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">right winger</a>, Beckham was runner up in the <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d\'Or</a>, twice runner-up for <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Player_of_the_Year" title="FIFA World Player of the Year">FIFA World Player of the Year</a> and in 2004 was named by <a href="/wiki/Pel%C3%A9" title="Pel\xc3\xa9">Pel\xc3\xa9</a> in the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_100" title="FIFA 100">FIFA 100</a> list of the world\'s greatest living players.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He was inducted into the <a href="/wiki/English_Football_Hall_of_Fame" title="English Football Hall of Fame">English Football Hall of Fame</a> in 2008. A global ambassador for the sport, Beckham is regarded as a <a href="/wiki/British_culture" class="mw-redirect" title="British culture">British cultural icon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham\'s professional club career began with Manchester United, where he made his first-team debut in 1992 aged 17.<sup id="cite_ref-galaxybio_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-galaxybio-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> With United, he won the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> title six times, the <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> twice, and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> in 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-galaxybio_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-galaxybio-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He then played four seasons with Real Madrid,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> winning the <a href="/wiki/La_Liga" title="La Liga">La Liga</a> championship in his final season with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> In July 2007 Beckham signed a five-year contract with <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a> club LA Galaxy.<sup id="cite_ref-Bandini_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Bandini-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> While a Galaxy player, he spent two loan spells in Italy with Milan in 2009 and 2010. He was the first British footballer to play 100 UEFA Champions League games.<sup id="cite_ref-galaxybio_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-galaxybio-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In international football, Beckham made his England debut on 1 September 1996 at the age of 21. He was <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captain</a> for <a href="/wiki/List_of_England_national_football_team_captains" title="List of England national football team captains">six years</a>, earning 58 caps during his tenure.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> He made 115 career appearances in total, appearing at three <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> tournaments, in <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998</a>, <a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002</a> and <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006</a>, and two <a href="/wiki/UEFA_European_Championship" title="UEFA European Championship">UEFA European Championship</a> tournaments, in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2000" title="UEFA Euro 2000">2000</a> and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2004" title="UEFA Euro 2004">2004</a>.\n</p><p>Beckham has consistently ranked among the highest earners in football, and in 2013 was listed as the highest-paid player in the world, having earned over $50&#160;million in the previous 12 months.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> He has been married to <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham" title="Victoria Beckham">Victoria Beckham</a> since 1999 and they have four children.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He has been a <a href="/wiki/UNICEF_UK" title="UNICEF UK">UNICEF UK</a> ambassador since 2005, and in 2015 he launched <i>7: The David Beckham UNICEF Fund</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-UNICEF_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNICEF-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, MLS announced that Beckham and a group of investors would own an <a href="/wiki/Inter_Miami_CF" title="Inter Miami CF">Inter Miami CF</a>, which will begin in 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-Miami_Beckham_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Miami_Beckham-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div id="toc" class="toc"><input type="checkbox" role="button" id="toctogglecheckbox" class="toctogglecheckbox" style="display:none" /><div class="toctitle" lang="en" dir="ltr"><h2>Contents</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-1 href="#Records"><span class="tocnumber">11</span> <span class="toctext">Records</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-32"><a href="#Tattoos"><span class="tocnumber">12</span> <span class="toctext">Tattoos</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-33"><a href="#Awards"><span class="tocnumber">13</span> <span class="toctext">Awards</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-34"><a href="#Career_statistics"><span class="tocnumber">14</span> <span class="toctext">Career statistics</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-35"><a href="#Club"><span class="tocnumber">14.1</span> <span class="toctext">Club</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-36"><a href="#International"><span class="tocnumber">14.2</span> <span class="toctext">International</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-37"><a href="#International_goals"><span class="tocnumber">14.3</span> <span class="toctext">International goals</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-38"><a href="#Honours"><span class="tocnumber">15</span> <span class="toctext">Honours</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-39"><a href="#Club_2"><span class="tocnumber">15.1</span> <span class="toctext">Club</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-40"><a href="#Individual"><span class="toctext">Orders and special awards</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-42"><a href="#Records_2"><span class="tocnumber">15.4</span> <span class="toclevel-1 tocsection-44"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">17</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a>\n<ul>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-45"><a href="#Books"><span class="tocnumber">17.1</span> <span class="toctext">Books</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-46"><a href="#Internet"><span class="tocnumber">17.2</span> <span class="toctext">Internet</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-47"><a href="#Further_reading"><span class="tocnumber">18</span> <span class="toctext">Further reading</span></a></li>\n<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-48"><a href="#External_links"><span class="tocnumber">19</span> <span class="toctext">External links</span></a></li>\n</ul>\n</div>\n\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span></h2>\n<p>Beckham was born at <a href="/wiki/Whipps_Cross_University_Hospital" title="Whipps Cross University Hospital">Whipps Cross University Hospital</a> in <a href="/wiki/Leytonstone" title="Leytonstone">Leytonstone</a>, London, England.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He is the son of Sandra Georgina (n\xc3\xa9e West; b. 1949), a hairdresser, and David Edward Alan "Ted" Beckham (b. <a href="/wiki/Edmonton,_London" title="Edmonton, London">Edmonton, London</a>, July\xe2\x80\x93September 1948), a kitchen fitter, who married at the <a href="/wiki/London_Borough_of_Hackney" title="London Borough of Hackney">London Borough of Hackney</a> in 1969.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> He has an older sister, Lynne Georgina, and a younger sister, Joanne Louise. He regularly played football in Ridgeway Park, <a href="/wiki/Chingford" title="Chingford">Chingford</a>, as a child, and attended Chase Lane Primary School and <a href="/wiki/Chingford_Foundation_School" title="Chingford Foundation School">Chingford County High School</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> In a 2007 interview, Beckham said that, "At school whenever the teachers asked, \'What do you want to do when you\'re older?\' I\'d say, \'I want to be a footballer.\' And they\'d say, \'No, what do you really want to do, for a job?\' But that was the only thing I ever wanted to do."<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> Beckham\'s maternal grandfather was <a href="/wiki/Jewish" class="mw-redirect" title="Jewish">Jewish</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> and Beckham has referred to himself as "half Jewish"<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> and wrote in his autobiography "I\'ve probably had more contact with Judaism than with any other religion".<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> In his book <i>Both Feet on the Ground</i>, he stated that growing up he attended church every week with his parents, because that was the only way he could play football for their team.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>His parents were fanatical <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> supporters who frequently travelled to <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a> from London to attend the team\'s home matches. David inherited his parents\' love of Manchester United, and his main sporting passion was football. He attended one of <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Charlton" title="Bobby Charlton">Bobby Charlton</a>\'s football schools in <a href="/wiki/Manchester" title="Manchester">Manchester</a> and won the chance to take part in a training session with <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, as part of a talent competition. He played for a local youth team called Ridgeway Rovers&#160;, which was coached by his father, Stuart Underwood, and Steve Kirby. Beckham was a Manchester United mascot for a match against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a> in 1986. Young Beckham had trials with his local club <a href="/wiki/Leyton_Orient_F.C." title="Leyton Orient F.C.">Leyton Orient</a>, <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a> and attended <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>\'s school of excellence. Tottenham Hotspur was the first club he played for. During a two-year period in which Beckham played for <a href="/wiki/Brimsdown_Rovers_F.C." title="Brimsdown Rovers F.C.">Brimsdown Rovers</a>\' youth team, he was named Under-15 Player of the Year in 1990.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He also attended Bradenton Preparatory Academy, but signed schoolboy forms at Manchester United on his 14th birthday, and subsequently signed a <a href="/wiki/Youth_Training_Scheme" title="Youth Training Scheme">Youth Training Scheme</a> contract on 8 July 1991.<sup id="cite_ref-YTS_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-YTS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manchester_United">Manchester United</span></h3>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth_and_early_career">Youth and early career</span></h4>\n<p>Having signed for Manchester United as a trainee on 8 July 1991,<sup id="cite_ref-H2G2_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-H2G2-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Beckham was part of a group of young players, including <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Giggs" title="Ryan Giggs">Ryan Giggs</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gary_Neville" title="Gary Neville">Gary Neville</a>, <a href="/wiki/Phil_Neville" title="Phil Neville">Phil Neville</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nicky_Butt" title="Nicky Butt">Nicky Butt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paul_Scholes" title="Paul Scholes">Paul Scholes</a>, who were coached by <a href="/wiki/Eric_Harrison_(footballer)" title="Eric Harrison (footballer)">Eric Harrison</a>, and helped the club win the <a href="/wiki/FA_Youth_Cup" title="FA Youth Cup">FA Youth Cup</a> in <a href="/wiki/FA_Youth_Cup_Finals_of_the_1990s#1991/92:_Manchester_United_v._Crystal_Palace_(3-1_and_3-2,_6-3_Aggregate)" title="FA Youth Cup Finals of the 1990s">May 1992</a>. Beckham scored Manchester United\'s second goal in the 30th minute of their 3\xe2\x80\x931 first-leg win of the final against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a> on 14 April 1992. In the second leg on 15 May, Beckham played a full 90-minutes of the fixture which ended 3\xe2\x80\x932 in favour of Manchester United and 6\xe2\x80\x933 on aggregate. Beckham\'s impact led to a first-team debut on 23 September 1992, as a substitute for <a href="/wiki/Andrei_Kanchelskis" title="Andrei Kanchelskis">Andrei Kanchelskis</a> in a <a href="/wiki/Football_League_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Football League Cup">League Cup</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Brighton_%26_Hove_Albion_F.C." title="Brighton &amp; Hove Albion F.C.">Brighton &amp; Hove Albion</a>. Shortly afterwards, Beckham signed as a professional on 23 January 1993.<sup id="cite_ref-H2G2_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-H2G2-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Manchester United again reached the <a href="/wiki/FA_Youth_Cup_Finals_of_the_1990s#1992/93:_Leeds_United_v._Manchester_United_(2-0_and_2-1,_4-1_Aggregate)" title="FA Youth Cup Finals of the 1990s">final of the FA Youth Cup</a>, where they faced <a href="/wiki/Leeds_United_F.C." title="Leeds United F.C.">Leeds United</a>. The first leg was played on 10 May 1993, where Beckham started in Manchester United\'s 2\xe2\x80\x930 home loss but was replaced by substitute <a href="/wiki/Robbie_Savage" title="Robbie Savage">Robbie Savage</a>. In the second leg on 13 May 1993, Beckham played the full 90 minutes of Manchester United\'s 2\xe2\x80\x931 defeat, which gave Leeds United a 4\xe2\x80\x931 aggregate score. Beckham also received honours with the club\'s reserve team when the squad won the league in 1994. In September 1994, Beckham made his first full appearance in the club\'s first team against <a href="/wiki/Port_Vale_F.C." title="Port Vale F.C.">Port Vale</a> in a League Cup fixture. On 7 December 1994, Beckham made his <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> debut, scoring a goal in a 4\xe2\x80\x930 victory at home to <a href="/wiki/Galatasaray_S.K._(football)" title="Galatasaray S.K. (football)">Galatasaray</a> in the final game of the group stage. Despite the victory, however, they finished third out of four in their group, behind Barcelona.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span id="Preston_North_End_.28loan.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Preston_North_End_(loan)">Preston North End (loan)</span></h4>\n<p>Beckham then went to <a href="/wiki/Preston_North_End_F.C." title="Preston North End F.C.">Preston North End</a> on loan for part of the <a href="/wiki/1994%E2%80%9395_in_English_football" title="1994\xe2\x80\x9395 in English football">1994\xe2\x80\x9395 season</a> to get some first team experience. He impressed, scoring two goals in five appearances, notably scoring directly from a <a href="/wiki/Corner_kick" title="Corner kick">corner kick</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Manchester_United">Return to Manchester United</span></h4>\n<p>Beckham returned to Manchester and made his <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> debut for Manchester United on 2 April 1995, in a goalless draw against Leeds United. He played four times for United in the league that season, as they finished second behind <a href="/wiki/Blackburn_Rovers_F.C." title="Blackburn Rovers F.C.">Blackburn Rovers</a>, missing out on a third successive Premier League title by a single point. He was not in the squad for the <a href="/wiki/1995_FA_Cup_Final" title="1995 FA Cup Final">FA Cup final</a> with <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a> on 20 May, which United lost 1\xe2\x80\x930, leaving the club without a major trophy for the first time since 1989.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>United manager <a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Sir Alex Ferguson</a> had a great deal of confidence in the club\'s young players. Beckham was part of a group of young talents Ferguson brought into United in the 1990s (known as "<a href="/wiki/Fergie%27s_Fledglings" title="Fergie&#39;s Fledglings">Fergie\'s Fledglings</a>"), which included <a href="/wiki/Nicky_Butt" title="Nicky Butt">Nicky Butt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gary_Neville" title="Gary Neville">Gary</a> and <a href="/wiki/Phil_Neville" title="Phil Neville">Phil Neville</a>. When experienced players <a href="/wiki/Paul_Ince" title="Paul Ince">Paul Ince</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mark_Hughes" title="Mark Hughes">Mark Hughes</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Andrei_Kanchelskis" title="Andrei Kanchelskis">Andrei Kanchelskis</a> left the club after the end of the 1994\xe2\x80\x9395 season, his decision to let youth team players replace them instead of buying star players from other clubs (United had been linked with moves for players including <a href="/wiki/Darren_Anderton" title="Darren Anderton">Darren Anderton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Marc_Overmars" title="Marc Overmars">Marc Overmars</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Baggio" title="Roberto Baggio">Roberto Baggio</a>, but no major signings were made that summer), drew a great deal of criticism. The criticism increased when United started the season with a 3\xe2\x80\x931 defeat at <a href="/wiki/Aston_Villa_F.C." title="Aston Villa F.C.">Aston Villa</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> with Beckham scoring United\'s only goal of the game. However, United recovered from this early season defeat and the young players performed well.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham swiftly established himself as United\'s right-sided midfielder (rather than a right-winger in the style of his predecessor Andrei Kanchelskis) and helped them to win the Premier League title and <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> <a href="/wiki/Double_(association_football)" title="Double (association football)">double</a> that season, scoring the winner in the semi-final against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and also providing the <a href="/wiki/Corner_kick" title="Corner kick">corner</a> from which <a href="/wiki/Eric_Cantona" title="Eric Cantona">Eric Cantona</a> scored in the FA Cup Final. Beckham\'s first title medal had, for a while, looked like it would not be coming that season, as United were still 10 points adrift of leaders <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a> at the turn of the new year, but Beckham and his teammates had overhauled the <a href="/wiki/Tyneside" title="Tyneside">Tynesiders</a> at the top of the league by mid March and they remained top until the end of the season. Despite playing regularly and to a consistently high standard for Manchester United, Beckham did not break into the England squad before <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_1996" title="UEFA Euro 1996">Euro 1996</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:28%;&#32;;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r856303512">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" \xe2\x80\x9c ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" \xe2\x80\x9d ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:360px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{min-width:100%;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"It changed my life. The ball seemed to be in the air for hours and it all went quiet. Then the ball went in and it just erupted. I was on cloud nine. I just wanted to shake everybody\'s hand and be out on the pitch for an hour."</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94Beckham on the goal from the half-way line against Wimbledon in August 1996 that made him a household name.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>At the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/1996%E2%80%9397_in_English_football" title="1996\xe2\x80\x9397 in English football">1996\xe2\x80\x9397 season</a>, Beckham was given the number 10 shirt that had most recently been worn by Mark Hughes. On 17 August 1996 (the first day of the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> season), Beckham became something of a household name when he scored a spectacular goal in a match against <a href="/wiki/Wimbledon_F.C." title="Wimbledon F.C.">Wimbledon</a>. With United leading 2\xe2\x80\x930, Beckham noticed that Wimbledon\'s goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Neil_Sullivan" title="Neil Sullivan">Neil Sullivan</a> was standing a long way out of his goal, and hit a shot from the halfway line \xe2\x80\x93 60 yards out \xe2\x80\x93 that floated over the goalkeeper and into the net.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>His <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebration</a> for his 60-yard strike saw him raise his arms as usual, but he walked away smiling rather than run as he often would.<sup id="cite_ref-Sky_Beckham_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sky_Beckham-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> When Beckham scored the goal he was wearing <a href="/wiki/Adidas_Predator" title="Adidas Predator">Adidas Predator</a> boots.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> In a UK poll conducted by <a href="/wiki/Channel_4" title="Channel 4">Channel 4</a> in 2002, the British public voted the goal No.18 in the list of the <a href="/wiki/100_Greatest_Sporting_Moments" class="mw-redirect" title="100 Greatest Sporting Moments">100 Greatest Sporting Moments</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> In a 2016 <a href="/wiki/Sky_Sports" title="Sky Sports">Sky Sports</a> poll it was ranked the best opening day goal in Premier League history.<sup id="cite_ref-Sky_Beckham_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sky_Beckham-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> During the 1996\xe2\x80\x9397 season, Beckham became an automatic first-choice player at Manchester United, helping them to retain the Premier League championship, and was voted <a href="/wiki/PFA_Young_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Young Player of the Year">PFA Young Player of the Year</a> by his peers.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Manchester United started the <a href="/wiki/1997%E2%80%9398_in_English_football" title="1997\xe2\x80\x9398 in English football">1997\xe2\x80\x9398 season</a> well but erratic performances in the second half of the season saw United finish second behind <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg/220px-1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg" width="220" height="143" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg/330px-1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0a/1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg/440px-1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4184" data-file-height="2729" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:1999_FA_Cup_Final_Beckham_corner.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham preparing to take a corner kick for <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> during the <a href="/wiki/1999_FA_Cup_Final" title="1999 FA Cup Final">1999 FA Cup Final</a> at Wembley Stadium</div></div></div>\n<p>In the <a href="/wiki/1998%E2%80%9399_in_English_football" title="1998\xe2\x80\x9399 in English football">1998\xe2\x80\x9399 season</a>, he was part of the United team that won the <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a> of the Premier League, FA Cup and <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>, a unique feat in English football.<sup id="cite_ref-treble_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-treble-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> There had been speculation that the criticism that he had received after being sent off in the World Cup would lead to him leaving England, but Beckham decided to stay at Manchester United.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>To ensure they would win the Premier League title, United needed to win their final league match of the season, at home to Tottenham. There were reports suggesting that the opposition would allow themselves to be beaten to prevent their local rivals Arsenal from retaining the title, but Tottenham took an early lead in the match.<sup id="cite_ref-treble_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-treble-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Beckham scored the equaliser with a curling strike from 25 yards out into the top left corner of the goal and United went on to win the match and the league.<sup id="cite_ref-treble_46-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-treble-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham played in central midfield in United\'s win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> in the <a href="/wiki/1999_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="1999 UEFA Champions League Final">1999 UEFA Champions League Final</a>, since United\'s first string centre-midfielders Paul Scholes and <a href="/wiki/Roy_Keane" title="Roy Keane">Roy Keane</a> were suspended for the match.<sup id="cite_ref-treble_46-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-treble-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> United were losing the match 1\xe2\x80\x930 at the end of normal time, but won the trophy by scoring two goals in injury time. Both of the goals came from corners taken by Beckham.<sup id="cite_ref-treble_46-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-treble-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Those crucial assists, coupled with great performances over the rest of the season, led to him finishing runner up to <a href="/wiki/Rivaldo" title="Rivaldo">Rivaldo</a> for 1999\'s <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">European Footballer of the Year</a> and <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Player_of_the_Year" title="FIFA World Player of the Year">FIFA World Player of the Year</a> awards.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Despite Beckham\'s achievements in the 1998\xe2\x80\x9399 season, he was still unpopular among some opposition fans and journalists, and he was criticised after being sent off for a deliberate foul in Manchester United\'s <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Club_World_Cup" title="FIFA Club World Cup">World Club Championship</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Club_Necaxa" title="Club Necaxa">Necaxa</a>. It was suggested in the press that his wife was a bad influence on him, and that it might be in United\'s interests to sell him,<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> but his manager publicly backed him and he stayed at the club. During the 1999\xe2\x80\x932000 season, there was a talk of a transfer to <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> in Italy, but this never happened. Beckham helped United retain the Premier League title in <a href="/wiki/1999%E2%80%932000_in_English_football" title="1999\xe2\x80\x932000 in English football">1999\xe2\x80\x932000</a> by an 18-point margin, after being pushed by Arsenal and Leeds United for much of the season. United won their final 11 league games of the season, with Beckham scoring five goals during this run, with his last goal coming from a swerving shot from the edge of the penalty area in their final home game against Tottenham Hotspur.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>By the early 2000s, the relationship between Ferguson and Beckham had begun to deteriorate, possibly as a result of Beckham\'s fame and commitments away from football. In 2000, Beckham was given permission to miss training to look after his son Brooklyn, who had <a href="/wiki/Gastroenteritis" title="Gastroenteritis">gastroenteritis</a>, but Ferguson was furious when <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham" title="Victoria Beckham">Victoria Beckham</a> was photographed at a London Fashion Week event on the same night, claiming that Beckham would have been able to train if Victoria had looked after Brooklyn that day. He responded by fining Beckham the maximum amount that was permitted (two weeks\' wages \xe2\x80\x93 then \xc2\xa350,000) and dropping him for a crucial match against United\'s rivals Leeds United. He later criticised Beckham for this in his autobiography, claiming he had not been "fair to his teammates"<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Beckham had a good season for his club, though, and helped United to win the Premier League by a record margin.\n</p>\n<blockquote>\n<p>"He was never a problem until he got married. He used to go into work with the academy coaches at night time, he was a fantastic young lad. Getting married into that entertainment scene was a difficult thing \xe2\x80\x93 from that moment, his life was never going to be the same. He is such a big celebrity, football is only a small part."\' \xe2\x80\x93 Alex Ferguson speaking about Beckham\'s marriage in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n</blockquote>\n<p>He was a key player in United\'s third successive league title in <a href="/wiki/2000%E2%80%9301_in_English_football" title="2000\xe2\x80\x9301 in English football">2000\xe2\x80\x9301</a>, only the fourth time that any club had achieved three league titles in a row. He scored nine goals that season, all in the Premier League.\n</p><p>On 10 April 2002, Beckham was injured during a Champions League match against <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_de_La_Coru%C3%B1a" title="Deportivo de La Coru\xc3\xb1a">Deportivo de La Coru\xc3\xb1a</a>, breaking the second <a href="/wiki/Metatarsus" class="mw-redirect" title="Metatarsus">metatarsal</a> bone in his left foot. There was speculation in the British media that the injury might have been caused deliberately, as the player who had injured Beckham was Argentine <a href="/wiki/Aldo_Duscher" title="Aldo Duscher">Aldo Duscher</a>, and <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> and <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> were due to meet in that year\'s World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> The injury prevented Beckham from playing for United for the rest of the season and they missed out on the Premier League title to Arsenal (also being knocked out of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> by <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a> on away goals in the semi-finals), but he signed a three-year contract in May, following months of negotiations with the club, mostly concerning extra payments for his image rights. The income from his new contract, and his many endorsement deals, made him the highest-paid player in the world at the time.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Despite the injury, 2001\xe2\x80\x9302 was arguably Beckham\'s best season as a United player; he scored 11 goals in 28 league games, and a total of 16 goals in 42 games in all competitions, the best of his career.\n</p><p>Following an injury early in the <a href="/wiki/2002%E2%80%9303_in_English_football" title="2002\xe2\x80\x9303 in English football">2002\xe2\x80\x9303 season</a>, Beckham was unable to regain his place on the Manchester United team, with <a href="/wiki/Ole_Gunnar_Solskj%C3%A6r" title="Ole Gunnar Solskj\xc3\xa6r">Ole Gunnar Solskj\xc3\xa6r</a> having replaced him on the right side of midfield. His relationship with his manager deteriorated further on 15 February 2003 when, in the changing room following an FA Cup defeat to Arsenal, a furious Alex Ferguson threw<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>\n<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> or kicked a <a href="/wiki/Football_boot" title="Football boot">boot</a> that struck Beckham over the eye, causing a cut that required stitches. The incident led to a great deal of transfer speculation involving Beckham, with <a href="/wiki/Bookmaker" title="Bookmaker">bookmakers</a> offering odds on whether he or Ferguson would be first to leave the club.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Although the team had started the season badly, their results improved greatly from December onwards and they won the league, with Beckham managing a total of 11 goals in 52 games in all competitions. He was still a first-choice player for England, however, and was appointed an <a href="/wiki/Officer_of_the_Most_Excellent_Order_of_the_British_Empire" class="mw-redirect" title="Officer of the Most Excellent Order of the British Empire">Officer of the Most Excellent Order of the British Empire</a> (OBE) for services to football on 13 June 2003.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham had made 265 Premier league appearances for United and scored 61 goals. He also made 81 Champions league appearances, scoring 15 goals. Beckham won six Premier League titles, two FA Cups, one <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">European Cup</a>, one Intercontinental Cup and one FA Youth Cup in the space of 12 years. By this stage, he was their joint second longest serving player behind <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Giggs" title="Ryan Giggs">Ryan Giggs</a> (having joined them at the same time as <a href="/wiki/Nicky_Butt" title="Nicky Butt">Nicky Butt</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gary_Neville" title="Gary Neville">Gary Neville</a> and <a href="/wiki/Paul_Scholes" title="Paul Scholes">Paul Scholes</a>).\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Real_Madrid">Real Madrid</span></h3>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:28%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He is a great player who is going to become part of the club\'s great history. He is a man of our times and a symbol of modern-day stardom and what is certain is <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a> have signed Beckham because he\'s a great footballer and a very dedicated professional. His team spirit is unsurpassed and he is one of the best English players of all-time and if only because of that he is with us."</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94Real Madrid President <a href="/wiki/Florentino_P%C3%A9rez" title="Florentino P\xc3\xa9rez">Florentino P\xc3\xa9rez</a> during Beckham\'s unveiling.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>As the summer 2003 transfer window approached, Manchester United appeared keen to sell Beckham to <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> and the two clubs even announced that they reached a deal for Beckham\'s transfer,<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> but instead he joined reigning Spanish champions <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a> for \xe2\x82\xac37&#160;million on a four-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> Beckham was the latest signing in the <i><a href="/wiki/Gal%C3%A1cticos" title="Gal\xc3\xa1cticos">Gal\xc3\xa1cticos</a></i> era of global stars signed by club president <a href="/wiki/Florentino_P%C3%A9rez" title="Florentino P\xc3\xa9rez">Florentino P\xc3\xa9rez</a> every summer.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> The news came as a bitter blow to the newly elected Barcelona president <a href="/wiki/Joan_Laporta" title="Joan Laporta">Joan Laporta</a>, who based much of his presidential campaign on signing Beckham.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> Though announced in mid-June, the transfer was completed on 1 July 2003, making him the third Englishman to play for the club, after <a href="/wiki/Laurie_Cunningham" title="Laurie Cunningham">Laurie Cunningham</a> and <a href="/wiki/Steve_McManaman" title="Steve McManaman">Steve McManaman</a>. Following a successful medical on 2 July, Beckham was unveiled in front of 500 accredited journalists from 25 countries at Real\'s basketball facility, where he was handed the famous white shirt by club legend <a href="/wiki/Alfredo_Di_St%C3%A9fano" title="Alfredo Di St\xc3\xa9fano">Alfredo Di St\xc3\xa9fano</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> Although Beckham had worn the number seven shirt for Manchester United and England, he was unable to wear it at Madrid as it was assigned to club captain <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_(footballer)" title="Ra\xc3\xbal (footballer)">Ra\xc3\xbal</a>. He decided to wear number 23 instead, citing his admiration of basketball player <a href="/wiki/Michael_Jordan" title="Michael Jordan">Michael Jordan</a>, who also wore the number 23 shirt, as the reason behind his decision.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_zidane.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Beckham_zidane.jpg/170px-Beckham_zidane.jpg" width="170" height="406" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/be/Beckham_zidane.jpg/255px-Beckham_zidane.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/be/Beckham_zidane.jpg 2x" data-file-width="262" data-file-height="625" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_zidane.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham (top) and <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a> at Real Madrid in August 2003</div></div></div>\n<p>In the week before Beckham\'s presentation, Real named <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Queiroz" title="Carlos Queiroz">Carlos Queiroz</a> as their new head coach, meaning that Beckham was reunited with a familiar face upon arriving to Madrid, since Queiroz had spent the previous season as Alex Ferguson\'s assistant at Manchester United. In late July 2003, the club went on a tour of the Far East as part of pre-season training, but also to cash in on Beckham\'s huge marketing appeal in Asia, where he enjoyed tremendous following. Real\'s brand recognition in that part of the globe was already well established as the club made financially successful trips to Asia during previous off-seasons. The presence of a global marketing icon such as Beckham, however, made this particular tour a financial smash for <i>los Merengues</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Shortly after his transfer to Real, Beckham also ended his relationship with agent Tony Stephens of <a href="/wiki/Live_Nation_Entertainment" title="Live Nation Entertainment">SFX Europe</a>, who had guided him through his career until that point, including helping to engineer Beckham\'s move from Manchester to Madrid. Beckham signed on with <a href="/wiki/Simon_Fuller" title="Simon Fuller">Simon Fuller</a> and his company <a href="/wiki/19_Entertainment" title="19 Entertainment">19 Entertainment</a>, which already managed the career of Victoria.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Beckham also appointed close friend <a href="/wiki/Terry_Byrne" title="Terry Byrne">Terry Byrne</a> to be his personal manager.<sup id="cite_ref-galaxy-millions_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-galaxy-millions-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:28%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"We knew before he was a good player, but we did not expect him to be such an influential player, to show such commitment to the team spirit. The way he runs for everything, the way he tries his best. He has everyone\'s respect."</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94<a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> speaking about Beckham in October 2003.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>In late August 2003, Real Madrid won the <a href="/wiki/2003_Supercopa_de_Espa%C3%B1a" title="2003 Supercopa de Espa\xc3\xb1a">Spanish Super Cup</a> over two legs versus <a href="/wiki/RCD_Mallorca" title="RCD Mallorca">RCD Mallorca</a>, with Beckham scoring the final goal in a 3\xe2\x80\x930 return leg win at home, thus setting the stage for the start of the league season. Playing in a star-laden team which included three former <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Player_of_the_Year" title="FIFA World Player of the Year">FIFA World Player of the Year</a> recipients, <a href="/wiki/Zinedine_Zidane" title="Zinedine Zidane">Zinedine Zidane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lu%C3%ADs_Figo" title="Lu\xc3\xads Figo">Lu\xc3\xads Figo</a>, in addition to <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Carlos" title="Roberto Carlos">Roberto Carlos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_(footballer)" title="Ra\xc3\xbal (footballer)">Ra\xc3\xbal</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iker_Casillas" title="Iker Casillas">Iker Casillas</a>, Beckham did not require much time to settle in, scoring five times in his first 16 matches (including a goal less than three minutes into his La Liga debut). Queiroz mostly favoured the adaptable 5\xe2\x80\x933\xe2\x80\x932 formation, with two fullbacks <a href="/wiki/M%C3%ADchel_Salgado" title="M\xc3\xadchel Salgado">M\xc3\xadchel Salgado</a> and <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Carlos" title="Roberto Carlos">Roberto Carlos</a>, often joining the attack down the wings, while Beckham played on the right of the three-man midfield, alongside Zidane and Figo.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Real Madrid were runners-up in the <a href="/wiki/2003%E2%80%9304_Copa_del_Rey" title="2003\xe2\x80\x9304 Copa del Rey">Copa del Rey</a>, were knocked out of the UEFA Champions League at the quarter-final stage and finished the league season in fourth place, meaning the team, whose president P\xc3\xa9rez expected them to win either the Spanish league or the Champions League each season, did not match expectations. In July 2004, while Beckham was in pre-season training in Spain, an intruder scaled a wall at the Beckham home while carrying a can of <a href="/wiki/Gasoline" title="Gasoline">petrol</a>. Victoria and their children were in the house at the time, but security guards apprehended the man before he reached the house.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The league season began with new head coach <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Antonio_Camacho" title="Jos\xc3\xa9 Antonio Camacho">Jos\xc3\xa9 Antonio Camacho</a> at the helm, but he ended up lasting only three matches, handing in his resignation as Real dropped to eighth spot in the La Liga standings. Camacho\'s assistant <a href="/wiki/Mariano_Garc%C3%ADa_Rem%C3%B3n" title="Mariano Garc\xc3\xada Rem\xc3\xb3n">Mariano Garc\xc3\xada Rem\xc3\xb3n</a> took over on temporary basis as Real\'s leadership scrambled to find a permanent replacement. Beckham made more headlines on 9 October 2004 when he admitted intentionally fouling <a href="/wiki/Ben_Thatcher" title="Ben Thatcher">Ben Thatcher</a> in an England match against <a href="/wiki/Wales_national_football_team" title="Wales national football team">Wales</a> to get himself booked. Beckham was due to receive a one-match suspension for his next <a href="/wiki/Yellow_card_(sports)" class="mw-redirect" title="Yellow card (sports)">caution</a>, and had picked up an injury which he knew would keep him out of England\'s next match, so he deliberately fouled Thatcher to serve his suspension in a match that he would have had to miss anyway. <a href="/wiki/The_Football_Association" title="The Football Association">The Football Association</a> asked Beckham for an explanation of his actions and he admitted that he had "made a mistake" and apologised.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> He was sent off shortly afterwards, this time in a league match for Real Madrid against <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>. Having received a <a href="/wiki/Misconduct_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Misconduct (football)">yellow card</a>, he was judged to have sarcastically applauded the referee and was given a second yellow card, causing an automatic dismissal, although the suspension was cancelled on appeal.\n</p><p>By Christmas 2004, with the team sitting in second position in the league, Garc\xc3\xada Rem\xc3\xb3n was dismissed, and <a href="/wiki/Vanderlei_Luxemburgo" title="Vanderlei Luxemburgo">Vanderlei Luxemburgo</a> became the new head coach. However, the well-travelled Brazilian failed to inspire the team to the title as Real again finished the season in second position. On 3 December 2005, Beckham was sent off for the third time that season in a league match against <a href="/wiki/Getafe_CF" title="Getafe CF">Getafe CF</a>. A day later Luxemburgo was sacked and was replaced by <a href="/wiki/Juan_Ram%C3%B3n_L%C3%B3pez_Caro" title="Juan Ram\xc3\xb3n L\xc3\xb3pez Caro">Juan Ram\xc3\xb3n L\xc3\xb3pez Caro</a>. By the end of that season, Beckham led La Liga in number of assists.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_warmingup.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Beckham_warmingup.jpg/170px-Beckham_warmingup.jpg" width="170" height="197" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Beckham_warmingup.jpg/255px-Beckham_warmingup.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Beckham_warmingup.jpg/340px-Beckham_warmingup.jpg 2x" data-file-width="558" data-file-height="648" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_warmingup.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham warming up with Real Madrid in August 2006</div></div></div>\n<p>During the season, Beckham established football academies in Los Angeles and east London and was named a judge for the 2006 British Book Awards.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> \nReal Madrid finished second to Barcelona in the 2005\xe2\x80\x9306 La Liga, albeit with a large 12-point gap, and only reached the last 16 in the Champions League after losing to Arsenal. The season also marked the end of an era for the club as P\xc3\xa9rez resigned his post as president in January 2006, with <a href="/wiki/Vicente_Boluda" title="Vicente Boluda">Vicente Boluda</a> named as replacement on an interim basis until the end of the season.\n</p><p>The summer 2006 off-season marked a turbulent time as the club\'s presidential elections were held. <a href="/wiki/Ram%C3%B3n_Calder%C3%B3n" title="Ram\xc3\xb3n Calder\xc3\xb3n">Ram\xc3\xb3n Calder\xc3\xb3n</a> became the new Real president. As expected, none of the club officials who served under the previous president was kept, including head coach L\xc3\xb3pez Caro. Initially out of favour with newly arrived head coach <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Capello" title="Fabio Capello">Fabio Capello</a>, Beckham started only a few games at the beginning of the season, as the speedier <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Antonio_Reyes" title="Jos\xc3\xa9 Antonio Reyes">Jos\xc3\xa9 Antonio Reyes</a> was normally preferred on the right wing. Of the first nine matches Beckham started, Real lost seven. On 10 January 2007, after prolonged contractual negotiations, Real Madrid\'s sporting director <a href="/wiki/Predrag_Mijatovi%C4%87" title="Predrag Mijatovi\xc4\x87">Predrag Mijatovi\xc4\x87</a> announced that Beckham would not remain at Real Madrid after the end of the season. However, he later claimed that he was mistranslated and that he actually said that Beckham\'s contract had not yet been renewed.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>On 11 January 2007, Beckham announced that he had signed a five-year deal to play for the <a href="/wiki/LA_Galaxy" title="LA Galaxy">LA Galaxy</a> beginning 1 July 2007. On 13 January 2007, Fabio Capello said that Beckham had played his last game for Real Madrid, although he continued to train with the team.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> A few days later, while speaking to the students at Villanueva University Center in Madrid, Calder\xc3\xb3n said that Beckham is "going to Hollywood to be half a film star", adding "our technical staff were right not to extend his contract, which has been proved by the fact that no other technical staff in the world wanted him except Los Angeles".<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>About a month later, however, Capello backtracked on his earlier statement, allowing Beckham to rejoin the team for the match against <a href="/wiki/Real_Sociedad" title="Real Sociedad">Real Sociedad</a> on 10 February 2007. The player immediately repaid his head coach\'s trust by scoring the equalising goal from a 27-yard free kick, as Real Madrid eventually recorded a 2\xe2\x80\x931 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> In his final UEFA Champions League appearance for the club, Real Madrid were knocked out of the competition by Bayern Munich at the <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_stage" title="2006\xe2\x80\x9307 UEFA Champions League knockout stage">round-of-16 stage</a> (on the away goals rule) on 7 March 2007. Beckham played a pivotal role in all three Madrid goals in the home game, with Bayern goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Oliver_Kahn" title="Oliver Kahn">Oliver Kahn</a> describing his performance as "world class".<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_2_(2114756146).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Beckham_2_%282114756146%29.jpg/220px-Beckham_2_%282114756146%29.jpg" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Beckham_2_%282114756146%29.jpg/330px-Beckham_2_%282114756146%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/Beckham_2_%282114756146%29.jpg/440px-Beckham_2_%282114756146%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3014" data-file-height="2006" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_2_(2114756146).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham during his last season with Real Madrid</div></div></div>\n<p>On 17 June 2007, the last day of the La Liga season, Beckham started in his final match for the club, a 3\xe2\x80\x931 win over Mallorca which saw them clinch the title from Barcelona. With Real down 0\xe2\x80\x931, Beckham limped off the field and was replaced by Jos\xc3\xa9 Antonio Reyes, who scored two goals, leading the team to that season\'s <a href="/wiki/2006%E2%80%9307_La_Liga" title="2006\xe2\x80\x9307 La Liga">La Liga title</a>, their first since Beckham had signed with them and <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F.#Domestic_competitions" title="Real Madrid C.F.">30th overall in the club\'s history</a>. Although Real and Bar\xc3\xa7elona both finished level on points, Madrid took the title because of their superior head-to-head record, capping a remarkable six-month turnaround for Beckham.<sup id="cite_ref-Liga_85-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liga-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> With his wife and children, along with celebrity friends <a href="/wiki/Tom_Cruise" title="Tom Cruise">Tom Cruise</a> and <a href="/wiki/Katie_Holmes" title="Katie Holmes">Katie Holmes</a>, watching from a luxury box at the <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Bernab%C3%A9u_Stadium" title="Santiago Bernab\xc3\xa9u Stadium">Santiago Bernab\xc3\xa9u Stadium</a>, it was only Beckham\'s second piece of silverware since he joined the famous club.<sup id="cite_ref-Liga_85-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Liga-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Towards the end of the season, as Beckham was getting back into Capello\'s good books after successfully fighting his way back into the first team, Real Madrid announced they would try to untie his transfer to LA Galaxy, but were ultimately unsuccessful.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> Several weeks before Beckham\'s scheduled arrival in the United States, Real\'s management contacted LA Galaxy\'s ownership group about reacquiring the player, but were quickly turned down.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>A month after the conclusion of Beckham\'s Real career, <i><a href="/wiki/Forbes" title="Forbes">Forbes</a></i> magazine reported that he had been the party primarily responsible for the team\'s huge increase in merchandise sales, a total reported to top US$600&#160;million during Beckham\'s four years at the club.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="LA_Galaxy">LA Galaxy</span></h3>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:20%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style=""><i>I\'m coming there not to be a superstar. I\'m coming there to be part of the team, to work hard and to hopefully win things. With me, it\'s about football. I\'m coming there to make a difference. I\'m coming there to play football&#160;... I\'m not saying me coming over to the States is going to make soccer the biggest sport in America. That would be difficult to achieve. Baseball, basketball, American football, they\'ve been around. But I wouldn\'t be doing this if I didn\'t think I could make a difference.</i><sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup></div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">Beckham on going to America<br /></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>Beckham\'s involvement with <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a> (MLS) began while he was still a Real Madrid player when it was confirmed on 11 January 2007 that he would be leaving Madrid in six months to join MLS side <a href="/wiki/LA_Galaxy" title="LA Galaxy">LA Galaxy</a>. The speculation about his new contract in Madrid was thus put to an end and the following day Beckham\'s official press conference was held in conjunction with the <a href="/wiki/2007_MLS_SuperDraft" title="2007 MLS SuperDraft">2007 MLS SuperDraft</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg/220px-Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg/330px-Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg/440px-Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg 2x" data-file-width="504" data-file-height="336" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_first_goal_LA_Galaxy.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham scores his first goal for LA Galaxy with a trademark free-kick.</div></div></div>\n<p>The announcement made top news all across the globe. Though many worldwide media outlets reported the deal to be worth US$250&#160;million,<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> the astronomical figure was soon revealed to be something of a PR stunt engineered by Beckham\'s media handlers (British representative agency <a href="/wiki/19_Entertainment" title="19 Entertainment">19 Entertainment</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> To maximise the media effect, in the press release they decided to list the potential sum that Beckham could make over the five-year period from all his revenue sources, which in addition to his Galaxy pay also include his personal endorsements. Beckham\'s actual deal with the Galaxy was a five-year contract worth US$32.5&#160;million in total or $6.5&#160;million per year.<sup id="cite_ref-galaxy-millions_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-galaxy-millions-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The high-profile acquisition paid immediate financial dividends for Galaxy long before Beckham joined the team. On the strength of the signing and the media frenzy it created, the club was able to pull off a new five-year shirt sponsorship deal with <a href="/wiki/Herbalife" class="mw-redirect" title="Herbalife">Herbalife</a> nutrition company worth US$20&#160;million. The gate revenue peaked as well with 11,000 new season tickets holders and sold-out luxury suites (each one of the 42 inside the team\'s home ground, the <a href="/wiki/StubHub_Center" title="StubHub Center">Home Depot Center</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.44_94-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.44-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> Even the LA Galaxy owners <a href="/wiki/Anschutz_Entertainment_Group" title="Anschutz Entertainment Group">Anschutz Entertainment Group</a> (AEG) saw an immediate spike in business. Involved on many business fronts worldwide, AEG was already leveraging its Beckham association in places such as China, where the company had been working aggressively in <a href="/wiki/Shanghai" title="Shanghai">Shanghai</a> and <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a> for years to receive clearance to build arenas and stadiums. The company\'s CEO <a href="/wiki/Tim_Leiweke" title="Tim Leiweke">Tim Leiweke</a> put it as follows: "Suddenly, we\'re known as the company that owns the team that David Beckham is going to play for, so our world changed".<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In the months following the announcement, the additional terms of Beckham\'s contract became public knowledge. One unique contract provision was giving him the option of buying an <a href="/wiki/Expansion_of_Major_League_Soccer" title="Expansion of Major League Soccer">MLS expansion</a> franchise in any market except New York City at the fixed price of $25&#160;million whenever he stopped playing in the league<sup id="cite_ref-Kennedy_96-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kennedy-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> \xe2\x80\x93 an allowance that the league\'s owners had never given to a player before. Another provision was the opt-out clause after the 2009 season, meaning that should he decide so, Beckham was free to leave the club after completing year three of his five-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.44_94-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.44-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> In April 2007, he and wife Victoria bought an $18.2&#160;million home on San Ysidro Drive in <a href="/wiki/Beverly_Hills" class="mw-redirect" title="Beverly Hills">Beverly Hills</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.66_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.66-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007.jpg/170px-David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007.jpg" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7b/David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007.jpg/255px-David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/7/7b/David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007.jpg 2x" data-file-width="300" data-file-height="450" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham (with a blue captain\'s armband) became LA Galaxy captain immediately upon joining the team</div></div></div>\n<p>Beckham\'s contract with LA Galaxy took effect on 11 July, and on 13 July, the famous Englishman was officially unveiled as a Galaxy player at the Home Depot Center to much fanfare and world media interest in front of more than 5,000 gathered fans and some 700 accredited media members.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> Beckham chose to wear number 23. It was announced that Galaxy jersey sales had already reached a record figure of over 250,000 prior to this formal introduction.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In parallel, Beckham\'s handlers at 19 Entertainment succeeded in putting together an unprecedented US media rollout designed to expand his carefully crafted personal brand in America. He made the cover of <i>Sports Illustrated</i>, a few weeks earlier <a href="/wiki/Adidas" title="Adidas">Adidas</a> launched the extensive 13-part ad campaign "F\xc3\xbatbol meets Football" starring Beckham and <a href="/wiki/National_Football_League" title="National Football League">NFL</a> running back <a href="/wiki/Reggie_Bush" title="Reggie Bush">Reggie Bush</a>, and <i>W</i> magazine published a racy photo spread featuring David and wife Victoria photographed by <a href="/wiki/Steven_Klein_(photographer)" class="mw-redirect" title="Steven Klein (photographer)">Steven Klein</a>. Meanwhile, ESPN sports network was running a promotional campaign and it also agreed to air <i>David Beckham: New Beginnings</i> documentary produced by 19 Entertainment before the friendly match versus <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, which was expected to be Beckham\'s American debut. In addition to popularising soccer, Beckham\'s arrival was used as platform for entertainment industry endeavours. Since both Beckham\'s and his wife\'s often overlapping careers were handled by 19 Entertainment, which is owned by <a href="/wiki/Simon_Fuller" title="Simon Fuller">Simon Fuller</a>, who in turn has a business relationship with the <a href="/wiki/Creative_Artists_Agency" title="Creative Artists Agency">Creative Artists Agency</a> (CAA), one of Hollywood\'s most powerful talent agencies, it was important also for CAA that the Beckhams made as big an impact as possible upon their arrival in the United States. On 16 July, CAA had hosted a welcoming bash for David at its new eight-storey, $400&#160;million headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Century_City" class="mw-redirect" title="Century City">Century City</a> with CAA employees reportedly instructed beforehand to line the staircase and clap for Beckham upon his arrival.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> That night Victoria\'s reality show prime-time special <i><a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham:_Coming_to_America" title="Victoria Beckham: Coming to America">Victoria Beckham: Coming to America</a></i> aired on NBC, drawing negative reviews in the press and poor viewership ratings.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007_Direction.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007_Direction.jpg/170px-David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007_Direction.jpg" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007_Direction.jpg/255px-David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007_Direction.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/e/e2/David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007_Direction.jpg 2x" data-file-width="300" data-file-height="450" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_Nov_11_2007_Direction.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham during a LA Galaxy game in November 2007</div></div></div>\n<p>On Saturday afternoon, 21 July, despite still nursing the injured left ankle that he picked up a month earlier during the final match of La Liga\'s season, Beckham made his Galaxy debut, coming on for <a href="/wiki/Alan_Gordon_(soccer)" title="Alan Gordon (soccer)">Alan Gordon</a> in the 78th minute of a 0\xe2\x80\x931 friendly loss to Chelsea as part of the <a href="/wiki/World_Series_of_Soccer_(MLS)" title="World Series of Soccer (MLS)">World Series of Soccer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> With a capacity crowd, along with a long Hollywood celebrity list featuring Tom Cruise, Katie Holmes, <a href="/wiki/Eva_Longoria" title="Eva Longoria">Eva Longoria</a>, <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_California" title="Governor of California">Governor of California</a> <a href="/wiki/Arnold_Schwarzenegger" title="Arnold Schwarzenegger">Arnold Schwarzenegger</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Drew_Carey" title="Drew Carey">Drew Carey</a> among others, present at the Home Depot Center, the match was broadcast live on ESPN\'s main network. However, the proceedings on the field of play took a back seat to the Beckham spectacle, and despite the presence of worldwide football stars such as <a href="/wiki/Andriy_Shevchenko" title="Andriy Shevchenko">Andriy Shevchenko</a>, <a href="/wiki/Didier_Drogba" title="Didier Drogba">Didier Drogba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Ballack" title="Michael Ballack">Michael Ballack</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Frank_Lampard" title="Frank Lampard">Frank Lampard</a>, the US television cameras were firmly focused on Beckham who spent most of the match on the bench. The match\'s added time featured a scare for already injured Beckham when he got tackled by <a href="/wiki/Steve_Sidwell" title="Steve Sidwell">Steve Sidwell</a> whose cleats struck Beckham\'s right foot, sending him airborne before he crumpled hard to the ground. Though the existing injury was not aggravated too much, Beckham\'s recovery process was set back by about a week. ESPN\'s presentation of Beckham\'s debut earned a 1.0 TV rating, meaning it was seen in an average of 947,000 television homes in the US \xe2\x80\x93 a disappointing figure given the national media buzz and two weeks of constant promotion by ESPN.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.66_97-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.66-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> As far as sporting events that were televised that weekend in the United States, Beckham\'s much publicised debut drew fewer TV viewers than <a href="/wiki/2007_Open_Championship" title="2007 Open Championship">British Open</a> golf tournament, a regular-season national baseball game, and even the <a href="/wiki/2007_IndyCar_Series_season" class="mw-redirect" title="2007 IndyCar Series season">Indy Racing League</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/2007_Honda_200" title="2007 Honda 200">Honda 200</a> motor race.<sup id="cite_ref-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.66_97-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-The_Beckham_Experiment_p.66-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The day after the made-for-TV debut was reserved for the welcoming party for the Beckhams at LA\'s <a href="/wiki/Museum_of_Contemporary_Art,_Los_Angeles" title="Museum of Contemporary Art, Los Angeles">Museum of Contemporary Art</a>, formally billed as being hosted by Tom Cruise, Katie Holmes, Will Smith, and Jada Pinkett Smith though in actuality a CAA-organized event. Attended by many Hollywood <a href="/wiki/A-list" title="A-list">A-listers</a>, the lavish bash was big news in the US celebrity tabloid media, including daily entertainment TV magazines such as <i><a href="/wiki/Entertainment_Tonight" title="Entertainment Tonight">Entertainment Tonight</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Access_Hollywood" class="mw-redirect" title="Access Hollywood">Access Hollywood</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham missed the next four LA Galaxy matches \xe2\x80\x93 three in the <a href="/wiki/North_American_SuperLiga" title="North American SuperLiga">North American SuperLiga</a> and an MLS game away at <a href="/wiki/Toronto_FC" title="Toronto FC">Toronto FC</a> though he still made the trip with his teammates, sitting on the bench in street clothes. It was in Toronto on 5 August that the team got its first taste of what life would be like on the road with Beckham on the roster. Due to security concerns, it was the first time the team flew on a charter for a road match, rather than flying commercial (MLS normally forbids charter flights for away matches, claiming they provide competitive advantage, but in this case they made an exception due to the frenzy created around Beckham and resulting security issues). Also, instead of the usual MLS-mandated modest hotels, LA Galaxy stayed at the five-star <a href="/wiki/King_Edward_Hotel_(Toronto)" class="mw-redirect" title="King Edward Hotel (Toronto)">Le M\xc3\xa9ridien King Edward</a> in <a href="/wiki/Downtown_Toronto" title="Downtown Toronto">downtown Toronto</a> (an expense paid for by the local <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">Toronto</a> promoter), while the glitz and glamour continued with the velvet rope, red carpet party at the Ultra Supper Club with Beckham as the centerpiece guest.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg/170px-Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg" width="170" height="229" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg/255px-Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/18/Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg/340px-Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1388" data-file-height="1872" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckham_LA_Galaxy_cropped.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham playing for LA Galaxy in March 2008</div></div></div>\n<p>Two weeks after his 12-minute appearance against Chelsea, Beckham made his league debut as a substitute on 9 August away versus <a href="/wiki/D.C._United" title="D.C. United">D.C. United</a> in front of the sellout crowd of 46,686 (nearly three times the average D.C. United home crowd) at the <a href="/wiki/Robert_F._Kennedy_Memorial_Stadium" title="Robert F. Kennedy Memorial Stadium">RFK Stadium</a>, coming on for <a href="/wiki/Quavas_Kirk" title="Quavas Kirk">Quavas Kirk</a> in the 71st minute.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> Coming into the nationally televised match on ESPN, played under a heavy downpour with his team down a man and down a goal, Beckham left a mark during the remaining 20-plus minutes. He hit a long free kick that <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Pav%C3%B3n" title="Carlos Pav\xc3\xb3n">Carlos Pav\xc3\xb3n</a> failed to finish on for the equaliser, and then in the final minutes Beckham served a weighted through ball into <a href="/wiki/Landon_Donovan" title="Landon Donovan">Landon Donovan</a>\'s path that United\'s keeper <a href="/wiki/Troy_Perkins" title="Troy Perkins">Troy Perkins</a> managed to break up in the last moment \xe2\x80\x93 the Galaxy lost 1\xe2\x80\x930. The next match on the road trip was at <a href="/wiki/New_England_Revolution" title="New England Revolution">New England Revolution</a> and Beckham decided to sit it out, fearing further aggravating his ankle injury on the <a href="/wiki/Gillette_Stadium" title="Gillette Stadium">Gillette Stadium</a>\'s artificial surface.\n</p><p>Beckham returned to the pitch the following week, again facing D.C. United, in the <a href="/wiki/North_American_SuperLiga" title="North American SuperLiga">SuperLiga</a> semi-final on 15 August. During this game he had many firsts with the Galaxy; his first start, first yellow card and first game as team captain.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> He also scored his first goal for the team, from a free kick, and also made his first assist, for Landon Donovan in the second half. These goals gave the team a 2\xe2\x80\x930 victory, and a place in the <a href="/wiki/2007_North_American_SuperLiga" title="2007 North American SuperLiga">North American SuperLiga</a> final versus <a href="/wiki/C.F._Pachuca" title="C.F.
