Pachuca">Pachuca</a> on 29 August.\n</p><p>During the SuperLiga final against Pachuca, Beckham injured his right knee, with an <a href="/wiki/Magnetic_resonance_imaging" title="Magnetic resonance imaging">MRI</a> scan revealing that he had sprained his <a href="/wiki/Medial_collateral_ligament" title="Medial collateral ligament">medial collateral ligament</a> and would be out for six weeks. He returned to play in the final home match of the season. The Galaxy were eliminated from playoff contention on 21 October, in the final MLS match of the season, a 1\xe2\x80\x930 loss to the <a href="/wiki/Chicago_Fire_Soccer_Club" title="Chicago Fire Soccer Club">Chicago Fire</a>. Beckham played as a substitute in the match, bringing his season totals to eight matches played (5 league); one goal scored (0 league); and three assists (2 league). Beckham trained with Arsenal from 4 January 2008 for three weeks until he returned to the Galaxy for pre-season training.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Beckham scored his first league goal with the Galaxy on 3 April against the <a href="/wiki/San_Jose_Earthquakes" title="San Jose Earthquakes">San Jose Earthquakes</a> in the ninth minute.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> On 24 May 2008, the Galaxy defeated the <a href="/wiki/Sporting_Kansas_City" title="Sporting Kansas City">Kansas City Wizards</a> 3\xe2\x80\x931, giving the Galaxy their first winning record in two years and moving the club into first place in the Western Conference. In the match, Beckham scored an empty-net goal from 70&#160;yards out. The goal marked the second time in Beckham\'s career that he had scored from his own half, the other being a 1996-goal from the half-way line against <a href="/wiki/Wimbledon_F.C." title="Wimbledon F.C.">Wimbledon</a> at <a href="/wiki/Selhurst_Park" title="Selhurst Park">Selhurst Park</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> Overall, however, the Galaxy had a disappointing year, failing to qualify for the end-of-season play-offs.\n</p>\n<h4><span id="Milan_.28loan.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Milan_(loan)">Milan (loan)</span></h4>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_%28cropped%29.jpg" width="170" height="254" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1120" data-file-height="1672" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_at_Al_Saad_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham playing for <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a></div></div></div>\n<p>In 2008, Beckham\'s success in the England national team under <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Capello" title="Fabio Capello">Fabio Capello</a> led to speculation that he might return to Europe to retain match fitness for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification">World Cup qualifying matches</a> in 2009. On 30 October 2008, <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> announced that Beckham was to join them on <a href="/wiki/Loan_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Loan (football)">loan</a> from 7 January 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Despite this and other speculation, Beckham made it clear that the move in no way signalled his intent to leave MLS and announced his intent to return to the Galaxy in time for the start of the <a href="/wiki/2009_Major_League_Soccer_season" title="2009 Major League Soccer season">2009 season</a> in March.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> Many at Milan both within and outside of the club expressed serious reservations about the transfer, with it considered by some players no more than a marketing move.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham was unveiled at Milan\'s <a href="/wiki/Milanello" title="Milanello">training facility</a> by the club\'s chief executive <a href="/wiki/Adriano_Galliani" title="Adriano Galliani">Adriano Galliani</a> on 20 December 2008. The player chose the number 32 shirt previously worn by <a href="/wiki/Christian_Vieri" title="Christian Vieri">Christian Vieri</a>, as both the number 7 and 23 shirts were already used by <a href="/wiki/Alexandre_Pato" title="Alexandre Pato">Alexandre Pato</a> and club vice captain <a href="/wiki/Massimo_Ambrosini" title="Massimo Ambrosini">Massimo Ambrosini</a>, respectively. The day after his unveiling, Beckham was brought to <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a> where he got introduced to home fans by walking out on the pitch before the league match versus <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a> and proclaiming "Forza Milan" over the public address system.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> Afterwards, he and wife Victoria watched from a luxury box as Milan won 5\xe2\x80\x931.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:28%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"On the pitch, Beckham sees everything before everyone else. His vision of play is better now than during his time in Manchester. He is slower but much stronger tactically and technically. He is very intelligent and works a lot."</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94A.C. Milan coach <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a> on Beckham\'s condition at 33 years old.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>Playing on the squad led by the 26-year-old superstar <a href="/wiki/Kak%C3%A1" title="Kak\xc3\xa1">Kak\xc3\xa1</a> in addition to several other world-class players at or near the peak of their careers \xe2\x80\x93 28-year-old <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a>, and 29-year-old <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Pirlo" title="Andrea Pirlo">Andrea Pirlo</a> \xe2\x80\x93 as well as club veterans <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Maldini" title="Paolo Maldini">Paolo Maldini</a>, <a href="/wiki/Clarence_Seedorf" title="Clarence Seedorf">Clarence Seedorf</a>, Massimo Ambrosini, <a href="/wiki/Giuseppe_Favalli" title="Giuseppe Favalli">Giuseppe Favalli</a>, <a href="/wiki/Gianluca_Zambrotta" title="Gianluca Zambrotta">Gianluca Zambrotta</a>, <a href="/wiki/Filippo_Inzaghi" title="Filippo Inzaghi">Filippo Inzaghi</a> and Andriy Shevchenko, Beckham made his competitive debut for the <i>rossoneri</i> in Serie A as a starter away at <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a> on 11 January 2009, playing 89&#160;minutes of the 2\xe2\x80\x932 draw in front of 53,444 at the <a href="/wiki/Stadio_Olimpico" title="Stadio Olimpico">Stadio Olimpico</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> Playing his first competitive match in almost three months, Beckham gave a decent performance in right midfield alongside Pirlo. Though clearly lacking match fitness, occasionally struggling to keep up in a high-tempo match, Beckham put in enough useful crosses and corners to justify the coach <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a>\'s decision to play him from the start.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> In Beckham\'s home debut against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a> a week later, he turned in another understated performance on the right side of midfield before advancing into a more active central role in the second half thus effectively taking over Seedorf\'s role after the Dutchman was subbed off. Milan won 1\xe2\x80\x930 courtesy of Pato, but the 65,000+ San Siro crowd mostly focused on Kak\xc3\xa1, imploring him to stay.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>A noticeably older team, Ancelotti-coached Milan was proving a good fit for the 33-year-old Englishman. He scored his first goal in Serie A for Milan in a 4\xe2\x80\x931 victory over <a href="/wiki/Bologna_F.C._1909" title="Bologna F.C. 1909">Bologna</a> on 25 January, his third appearance for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> Though Beckham was expected to return to Los Angeles in March, after impressing at the Italian club, scoring two goals in his first four matches and assisting on several more, rumours began to swirl that Beckham would stay in Milan, with the Italian club reportedly offering to pay a multimillion-dollar fee for him. The rumours were confirmed on 4 February, when Beckham stated that he was seeking a permanent transfer to Milan in a bid to sustain his England career through the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a>. Milan, however, failed to match Galaxy\'s valuation of Beckham, in the US$10\xe2\x80\x9315&#160;million range.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Still, negotiations continued during a month of speculation.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> On 2 March, the <i><a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_Times" title="Los Angeles Times">Los Angeles Times</a></i> reported that Beckham\'s loan had been extended through mid-July.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> This was later confirmed by Beckham, revealing what was described as a unique "<a href="/wiki/Timeshare" title="Timeshare">timeshare</a>" deal, in which Beckham would play with L.A. from mid-July till the end of the 2009 MLS season.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Galaxy">Return to Galaxy</span></h3>\n<p>After his return from Milan, many LA fans showed dislike and anger towards him as he missed the first half of the season and several held up signs saying "Go home fraud", and "Part-time player".<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> The Galaxy, however, had <a href="/wiki/2009_Los_Angeles_Galaxy_season" title="2009 Los Angeles Galaxy season">a much more successful season</a> than in previous years, rising from third to first in the Western Conference during Beckham\'s time with them. He remained a key part of the squad which saw Galaxy win the 2009 <a href="/wiki/Western_Conference_(MLS)" title="Western Conference (MLS)">Western Conference final</a> after a 2\xe2\x80\x930 overtime victory over the <a href="/wiki/Houston_Dynamo" title="Houston Dynamo">Houston Dynamo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>\nIn the <a href="/wiki/2009_MLS_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="2009 MLS Cup">final</a> on 22 November 2009, the Galaxy lost to <a href="/wiki/Real_Salt_Lake" title="Real Salt Lake">Real Salt Lake</a> by 5\xe2\x80\x934 in a penalty shoot-out after a 1\xe2\x80\x931 draw. Beckham also scored in the shootout.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span id="Return_to_Milan_.28loan.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Milan_(loan)">Return to Milan (loan)</span></h4>\n<p>In November 2009, after the end of 2009 MLS season, it was confirmed that Beckham would return to Milan for a second loan period beginning in January 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> On 6 January 2010, Beckham made a winning return in a Milan shirt, playing 75&#160;minutes of a 5\xe2\x80\x932 victory over <a href="/wiki/Genoa_C.F.C." title="Genoa C.F.C.">Genoa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup> On 16 February 2010, Beckham played against Manchester United for the first time since he left the club in 2003. He played 76&#160;minutes of the match at the San Siro \xe2\x80\x93 which ended 3\xe2\x80\x932 to Manchester United \xe2\x80\x93 before being substituted for Clarence Seedorf.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham returned to Old Trafford for the second leg of the tie on 10 March 2010; he did not start the match, but was brought on for <a href="/wiki/Ignazio_Abate" title="Ignazio Abate">Ignazio Abate</a> in the 64th minute to a positive reception from the Manchester United fans. The score was 3\xe2\x80\x930 for United at that point and the tie was all but decided. The match was the first time Beckham had played against Manchester United at Old Trafford and saw him create several scoring opportunities via crosses and corner kicks, but Manchester United dominated Milan and beat them 4\xe2\x80\x930, winning the tie 7\xe2\x80\x932.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> Following the final whistle, he aroused a bit of controversy by draping the green-and-gold scarf around his neck that was given to him by the Manchester United supporters protesting against club owner <a href="/wiki/Malcolm_Glazer" title="Malcolm Glazer">Malcolm Glazer</a>. As the fan protests against Glazer by the people gathered around <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_Supporters%27_Trust" title="Manchester United Supporters&#39; Trust">Manchester United Supporters\' Trust</a> gained steam in 2010, the green-and-gold scarf had come to be seen as an anti-Glazer symbol, and by extension many saw Beckham\'s decision to publicly put it on as gesture of support. When asked about it later, however, Beckham responded that protests are not his business.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In Milan\'s next game, against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Chievo_Verona" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Chievo Verona">Chievo</a>, Beckham suffered a <a href="/wiki/Achilles_tendon_rupture" title="Achilles tendon rupture">torn left Achilles tendon</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> causing him to miss the World Cup as well as the <a href="/wiki/2010_Major_League_Soccer_season" title="2010 Major League Soccer season">MLS season</a> due to the injury, which took him out of action for the next five months. Doctor <a href="/wiki/Sakari_Orava" title="Sakari Orava">Sakari Orava</a> performed surgery on Beckham\'s tendon in <a href="/wiki/Turku" title="Turku">Turku</a>, Finland, on 15 March 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> After the operation, Orava affirmed that, "it went quite fine. The prognosis is he needs a rehabilitation for the next few months, and the plaster cast is the next six to eight weeks. I would say that [it will be] maybe four months before he\'s running, but six months before he\'s jumping and kicking."<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_return_to_Galaxy">Second return to Galaxy</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg/170px-David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg/255px-David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg/340px-David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1719" data-file-height="2574" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_2010_LA_Galaxy.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham in 2010</div></div></div>\n<p>On 11 September 2010, after recovering from his Achilles tendon injury, Beckham returned to the game as a substitute in the 70th minute in the Galaxy\'s 3\xe2\x80\x931 win over <a href="/wiki/Columbus_Crew" class="mw-redirect" title="Columbus Crew">Columbus Crew</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> On 4 October, Beckham scored a trademark free kick in a 2\xe2\x80\x931 win over <a href="/wiki/Chivas_USA" title="Chivas USA">Chivas USA</a> to mark his first goal in <a href="/wiki/2010_Major_League_Soccer_season" title="2010 Major League Soccer season">2010</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> On 24 October, Beckham scored his second goal of the season in the Galaxy\'s 2\xe2\x80\x931 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Dallas" title="FC Dallas">FC Dallas</a> which secured them their second successive <a href="/wiki/Western_Conference_(MLS)" title="Western Conference (MLS)">Western Conference</a> title and first <a href="/wiki/MLS_Supporters%27_Shield" class="mw-redirect" title="MLS Supporters&#39; Shield">MLS Supporters\' Shield</a> since <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer_2002_Season" class="mw-redirect" title="Major League Soccer 2002 Season">2002</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>During January and February 2011, ahead of the 2011 MLS season, Beckham trained with Tottenham Hotspur. Rumours in the media claimed that the club were in talks with the Galaxy to sign the player on loan, but, according to Spurs manager <a href="/wiki/Harry_Redknapp" title="Harry Redknapp">Harry Redknapp</a>, the move was blocked by Galaxy, who wanted a full final season from their number 23.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> As a result, he ended up only training with the club as he had done with Arsenal three years earlier. With Beckham playing in the centre of midfield, the Galaxy won the 2011 MLS cup.<sup id="cite_ref-MLS_final_139-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MLS_final-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="MLS_Cup_champion">MLS Cup champion</span></h4>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_2012.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/David_Beckham_2012.jpg/220px-David_Beckham_2012.jpg" width="220" height="188" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/David_Beckham_2012.jpg/330px-David_Beckham_2012.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/David_Beckham_2012.jpg/440px-David_Beckham_2012.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1817" data-file-height="1554" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_2012.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham with LA Galaxy in 2012</div></div></div>\n<p>On 15 May, Beckham scored his first goal of the season for the Galaxy from a 30-yard free kick, in a 4\xe2\x80\x931 victory over Sporting Kansas City.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> On 9 July, Beckham scored directly from a corner in a 2\xe2\x80\x931 win over Chicago Fire, repeating a feat he also achieved while playing for <a href="/wiki/Preston_North_End_F.C." title="Preston North End F.C.">Preston North End</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>After having his best season with the Galaxy to date and finishing second in the league in assists, Beckham finished his fifth MLS season on a high. On 20 November 2011, he joined an elite group of players to have won league titles in three countries, when Los Angeles won their third <a href="/wiki/MLS_Cup" title="MLS Cup">MLS Cup</a> against the Houston Dynamo, winning 1\xe2\x80\x930 on a goal by captain Landon Donovan, with assists from Beckham and fellow designated player <a href="/wiki/Robbie_Keane" title="Robbie Keane">Robbie Keane</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-MLS_final_139-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MLS_final-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Following the 2011 season, in which the Galaxy won their second consecutive <a href="/wiki/Supporters%27_Shield" title="Supporters&#39; Shield">Supporters\' Shield</a>, having the second most points in MLS history, Beckham\'s five-year contract with the Galaxy expired on 31 December 2011. Despite being 36, he stated that he did not intend to retire. Beckham was heavily linked with <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a>, but on 18 January 2012, Galaxy announced Beckham had signed a new two-year contract to remain in Los Angeles.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup> In May 2012, Beckham and his victorious teammates were received by <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> at the <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham helped the Galaxy to a fourth-place finish in the MLS Western Conference 2012 regular season with Beckham scoring seven goals and adding nine assists. The Galaxy defeated <a href="/wiki/Vancouver_Whitecaps_FC" title="Vancouver Whitecaps FC">Vancouver Whitecaps FC</a>, the San Jose Earthquakes, <a href="/wiki/Seattle_Sounders_FC" title="Seattle Sounders FC">Seattle Sounders FC</a> and then 3\xe2\x80\x931 over the Houston Dynamo to retain the <a href="/wiki/MLS_Cup_2012" title="MLS Cup 2012">MLS Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> He was subbed off in the 89th minute for <a href="/wiki/Marcelo_Sarvas" title="Marcelo Sarvas">Marcelo Sarvas</a> and was given a standing ovation at their home venue.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> Beckham had earlier announced that the <a href="/wiki/MLS_Cup_2012" title="MLS Cup 2012">2012 MLS Cup Final</a> would be his final game with the Galaxy despite having another year remaining on his contract.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paris_Saint-Germain_and_retirement">Paris Saint-Germain and retirement</span></h3>\n<p>On 31 January 2013, ahead of the transfer deadline it was announced that Beckham would be undergoing a medical with Paris Saint-Germain ahead of a potential move to the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> side.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> Beckham signed a five-month deal with the club later that afternoon and confirmed that his entire salary during his time in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> would be donated to a local children\'s charity.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> His PSG debut came on 24 February 2013, when he came off the bench in the 76th minute in a Ligue 1 home match against <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a>. This made him the 400th player in the history of the club.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> On 12 May 2013, Beckham won a fourth different top flight winners\' medal after PSG beat Lyon 1\xe2\x80\x930 to claim the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> title.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>On 16 May 2013, Beckham announced that he would retire from professional football at the end of that year\'s French football season.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> Following his decision to retire at the end of the 2012\xe2\x80\x9313 season, Beckham was given specially designed boots in the colours of the <a href="/wiki/Union_Jack" title="Union Jack">Union Jack</a> to wear in his final game. These boots had the names of his wife and children stitched on to them. On 18 May 2013, Beckham was made captain in his final home game against Brest.<sup id="cite_ref-PSG_158-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSG-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> In this game, Beckham assisted a goal by Matuidi from a corner. Beckham was subbed after 80 minutes, receiving hugs from his fellow players and manager, as well as a standing ovation from fans.<sup id="cite_ref-PSG_158-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSG-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> PSG went on to win the game 3\xe2\x80\x931.<sup id="cite_ref-PSG_158-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSG-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/David_Beckham.jpg/220px-David_Beckham.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/David_Beckham.jpg/330px-David_Beckham.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/David_Beckham.jpg/440px-David_Beckham.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2816" data-file-height="2112" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham as England captain</div></div></div>\n<p>Beckham made his first appearance for the <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England national team</a> on 1 September 1996, in a <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">World Cup</a> qualifying match against <a href="/wiki/Moldova_national_football_team" title="Moldova national football team">Moldova</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="1998_FIFA_World_Cup">1998 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>\n<p>Beckham had played in all of England\'s qualifying matches for the <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998 World Cup</a> and was part of the England squad at the World Cup finals in France,<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> but the team\'s manager <a href="/wiki/Glenn_Hoddle" title="Glenn Hoddle">Glenn Hoddle</a> publicly accused him of not concentrating on the tournament,<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> and he did not start in either of England\'s first two games. He was picked for the third game against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> and scored with a <a href="/wiki/Curl_(football)" title="Curl (football)">bending</a> 30-yard <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" title="Direct free kick">free kick</a> in a 2\xe2\x80\x930 victory, which was his first goal for England.<sup id="cite_ref-Colombia_162-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Colombia-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In the second round (last 16) of that competition, he received a <a href="/wiki/Misconduct_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Misconduct (football)">red card</a> in England\'s match against <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Argentina_163-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Argentina-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup> Beckham, after having been fouled by <a href="/wiki/Diego_Simeone" title="Diego Simeone">Diego Simeone</a>, kicked Simeone while lying on the floor, striking him on the calf muscle.<sup id="cite_ref-Argentina_163-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Argentina-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/Sports_Illustrated" title="Sports Illustrated">Sports Illustrated</a></i> was critical of the Argentinians\' theatrics in that incident, stating that Simeone first delivered a "heavy-handed challenge" on Beckham and then "fell like a ton of bricks" when Beckham retaliated.<sup id="cite_ref-sportsillustrated.cnn_July_1998_164-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sportsillustrated.cnn_July_1998-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> Simeone later admitted to trying to get Beckham sent off by over-reacting to the kick and then, along with other members of his team, urging the referee to send Beckham off.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> The match finished in a draw and England were eliminated in a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Penalty shootout (association football)">penalty shootout</a>. Many supporters and journalists blamed him for England\'s elimination and he became the target of criticism and abuse, including the hanging of an <a href="/wiki/Effigy" title="Effigy">effigy</a> outside a London <a href="/wiki/Public_house" class="mw-redirect" title="Public house">pub</a>, and the <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Mirror" title="Daily Mirror">Daily Mirror</a></i> printing a <a href="/wiki/Darts" title="Darts">dartboard</a> with a picture of him centred on the bullseye. Beckham also received death threats after the World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span id="Euro_2000.2C_and_England_captaincy"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2000,_and_England_captaincy">Euro 2000, and England captaincy</span></h3>\n<p>The abuse that Beckham was receiving from English supporters peaked during <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2000_Group_A#Portugal_vs_England" title="UEFA Euro 2000 Group A">England\'s 3\xe2\x80\x932 defeat</a> by <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2000" title="UEFA Euro 2000">Euro 2000</a>, a match where Beckham set up two goals, when a group of England supporters taunted him throughout the match.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> Beckham responded by <a href="/wiki/Finger_(gesture)" class="mw-redirect" title="Finger (gesture)">raising his middle finger</a> and, while the gesture attracted some criticism, many of the newspapers that had previously encouraged his vilification asked their readers to stop abusing him.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:28%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"We\'ve played two and a half minutes of stoppage time. England trail by 2 goals to 1. Beckham could raise the roof here with a goal&#160;... I don\'t believe it! David Beckham scores the goal to take England all the way to the World Cup Finals!&#160;... Give that man a Knighthood!"</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94Television commentary on Beckham\'s stoppage time 30-yard curling free-kick against Greece in the 2002 World Cup qualifying game in October 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>On 15 November 2000, following <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Keegan" title="Kevin Keegan">Kevin Keegan</a>\'s resignation as England manager in October, Beckham was promoted to team captain by the caretaker manager <a href="/wiki/Peter_Taylor_(footballer_born_1953)" class="mw-redirect" title="Peter Taylor (footballer born 1953)">Peter Taylor</a>, and then kept the role under new manager <a href="/wiki/Sven-G%C3%B6ran_Eriksson" title="Sven-G\xc3\xb6ran Eriksson">Sven-G\xc3\xb6ran Eriksson</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-captain_170-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-captain-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham played a major role in helping England qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002 FIFA World Cup</a>, starring in an impressive 5\xe2\x80\x931 victory over <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> in Munich. The final step in Beckham\'s conversion from villain to national hero happened in England\'s final qualifying game against <a href="/wiki/Greece_national_football_team" title="Greece national football team">Greece</a> on 6 October 2001.<sup id="cite_ref-Greece_171-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Greece-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> England needed to win or draw the match to qualify outright for the World Cup, but were losing 2\xe2\x80\x931 with little time remaining. When <a href="/wiki/Teddy_Sheringham" title="Teddy Sheringham">Teddy Sheringham</a> was fouled eight yards outside the Greek penalty area, England were awarded a free-kick and Beckham ensured England\'s qualification with a curling strike of the kind that had become his trademark.<sup id="cite_ref-Greece_171-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Greece-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> Beckham was voted the <a href="/wiki/BBC_Sports_Personality_of_the_Year" title="BBC Sports Personality of the Year">BBC Sports Personality of the Year</a> for 2001, and finished runner-up, to <a href="/wiki/Lu%C3%ADs_Figo" title="Lu\xc3\xads Figo">Lu\xc3\xads Figo</a> of Portugal, for the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Player_of_the_Year" title="FIFA World Player of the Year">FIFA World Player of the Year</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2002_FIFA_World_Cup">2002 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:020607beckhamPK.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/020607beckhamPK.jpg/220px-020607beckhamPK.jpg" width="220" height="141" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/020607beckhamPK.jpg/330px-020607beckhamPK.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/020607beckhamPK.jpg/440px-020607beckhamPK.jpg 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="320" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:020607beckhamPK.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham scoring a penalty against <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> at the 2002 World Cup</div></div></div>\n<p>Beckham was partially fit by the time of the <a href="/wiki/2002_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2002 FIFA World Cup">2002 World Cup</a> held in Japan and South Korea, and played in the first match against <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a>. After the events of four years earlier, Beckham achieved a degree of revenge over Argentina by scoring the winning goal with a penalty, causing Argentina to fail to qualify for the knockout stage.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> England defeated <a href="/wiki/Denmark_national_football_team" title="Denmark national football team">Denmark</a> in the second round with Beckham providing an assist in a 3\xe2\x80\x930 win. England were knocked out in the quarter-finals by eventual winners <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> after <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a> scored the winner.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The following month, at the opening ceremony of the <a href="/wiki/2002_Commonwealth_Games" title="2002 Commonwealth Games">2002 Commonwealth Games</a> in Manchester, Beckham escorted <a href="/wiki/Kirsty_Howard" title="Kirsty Howard">Kirsty Howard</a> as she presented the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Jubilee_of_Elizabeth_II" title="Golden Jubilee of Elizabeth II">Jubilee Baton to the Queen</a>. Beckham played in all of England\'s matches at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2004" title="UEFA Euro 2004">Euro 2004</a>. He had a penalty saved in England\'s 2\xe2\x80\x931 defeat to France and missed another in a <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shootout_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Penalty shootout (football)">penalty shootout</a> in the quarter-final match against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Euros_175-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Euros-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup> England lost the shootout thus going out of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-Euros_175-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Euros-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham became a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Children%27s_Fund" class="mw-redirect" title="United Nations Children&#39;s Fund">UNICEF</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_UNICEF_Goodwill_Ambassadors" title="List of UNICEF Goodwill Ambassadors">Goodwill Ambassador</a> in January 2005 and was involved in promoting London\'s successful bid for the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 Olympic Games</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> In October 2005, Beckham\'s sending off against <a href="/wiki/Austria_national_football_team" title="Austria national football team">Austria</a> made him the first England captain to be sent off and the first player to be sent off twice while playing for England. He captained England for the 50th time in a friendly international against Argentina the following month.<sup id="cite_ref-captain_170-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-captain-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2006_FIFA_World_Cup">2006 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>\n<p>In England\'s opening game at the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 World Cup</a>, against <a href="/wiki/Paraguay_national_football_team" title="Paraguay national football team">Paraguay</a> on 10 June 2006, Beckham\'s free kick led to an <a href="/wiki/Own-goal" class="mw-redirect" title="Own-goal">own-goal</a> by <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Gamarra" title="Carlos Gamarra">Carlos Gamarra</a> as England won 1\xe2\x80\x930. In England\'s next match, played against <a href="/wiki/Trinidad_and_Tobago_national_football_team" title="Trinidad and Tobago national football team">Trinidad and Tobago</a> on 15 June 2006, Beckham\'s cross in the 83rd minute led to a <a href="/wiki/Peter_Crouch" title="Peter Crouch">Peter Crouch</a> goal, which put England into the lead 1\xe2\x80\x930. Beckham gave another assist to <a href="/wiki/Steven_Gerrard" title="Steven Gerrard">Steven Gerrard</a>. In the end they won 2\xe2\x80\x930. He was named <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_Match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the Match">Man of the Match</a> by tournament sponsor <a href="/wiki/Budweiser" title="Budweiser">Budweiser</a>.\n</p><p>During England\'s second round match against <a href="/wiki/Ecuador_national_football_team" title="Ecuador national football team">Ecuador</a>, Beckham scored from a free kick in the 59th minute, becoming the first English player to score in three separate World Cups,<sup id="cite_ref-Ecuador_177-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ecuador-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> and giving England a 1\xe2\x80\x930 victory and a place in the quarter-finals. He was sick before the game and vomited several times as a result of <a href="/wiki/Dehydration" title="Dehydration">dehydration</a> and illness that he got after having scored the winning goal for England.<sup id="cite_ref-Ecuador_177-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ecuador-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> In the quarter-final against Portugal, Beckham was substituted following an injury shortly after half time and the England team went on to lose the match on penalties (3\xe2\x80\x931), the score having been 0\xe2\x80\x930 after extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> After his substitution, Beckham was visibly shaken and emotional for not being able to play, being in tears at one point.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>A day after England were knocked out of the World Cup, an emotional Beckham made a statement in a news conference that he had stepped down as England captain,<sup id="cite_ref-captain_170-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-captain-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> stating, "It has been an honour and privilege to captain my country but, having been captain for 58 of my 95<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> games, I feel the time is right to pass on the armband as we enter a new era under <a href="/wiki/Steve_McClaren" title="Steve McClaren">Steve McClaren</a>." (Beckham had won 94 <a href="/wiki/Cap_(sport)" title="Cap (sport)">caps</a> up to that point.) He was succeeded by <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> captain <a href="/wiki/John_Terry" title="John Terry">John Terry</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Having stepped down as captain after the World Cup, Beckham was dropped completely from the England national team selected by new coach <a href="/wiki/Steve_McClaren" title="Steve McClaren">Steve McClaren</a> on 11 August 2006. McClaren claimed that he was "looking to go in a different direction" with the team, and that Beckham "wasn\'t included within that."<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup> McClaren said Beckham could be recalled in future. <a href="/wiki/Shaun_Wright-Phillips" title="Shaun Wright-Phillips">Shaun Wright-Phillips</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kieran_Richardson" title="Kieran Richardson">Kieran Richardson</a>, and the World Cup alternative to Beckham, <a href="/wiki/Aaron_Lennon" title="Aaron Lennon">Aaron Lennon</a>, were all included, although McClaren eventually opted to employ <a href="/wiki/Steven_Gerrard" title="Steven Gerrard">Steven Gerrard</a> in that role.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Post_2006_World_Cup">Post 2006 World Cup</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg/220px-Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg" width="220" height="151" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg/330px-Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e5/Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg/440px-Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="413" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Beckhamtakesfreekick.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham takes the free kick against <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> from which <a href="/wiki/John_Terry" title="John Terry">John Terry</a> scored.</div></div></div>\n<p>On 26 May 2007, McClaren announced that Beckham would be recalled to the England squad for the first time since stepping down as their captain. Beckham started against <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> in England\'s first match at the new <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a> and put in a positive performance. In the second half, he set up England\'s goal converted by captain <a href="/wiki/John_Terry" title="John Terry">John Terry</a>. It looked as though England would claim victory over Brazil, but newcomer <a href="/wiki/Diego_Ribas_da_Cunha" class="mw-redirect" title="Diego Ribas da Cunha">Diego</a> equalised in the dying seconds. In England\'s next match, a Euro 2008 qualifier against <a href="/wiki/Estonia_national_football_team" title="Estonia national football team">Estonia</a>, Beckham sent two trademark assists for <a href="/wiki/Michael_Owen" title="Michael Owen">Michael Owen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Peter_Crouch" title="Peter Crouch">Peter Crouch</a>, helping England to prevail 3\xe2\x80\x930. Beckham had assisted in three of England\'s four total goals in those two games,<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup> and he stated his desire to continue to play for England after his move to <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a>.\n</p><p>On 22 August 2007, Beckham played in a friendly for England against <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a>, becoming the first to play for England while with a non-European club team.<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> On 21 November 2007, Beckham earned his 99th cap against <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a>, setting up a goal for Peter Crouch to tie the game at 2\xe2\x80\x932. Following the 2\xe2\x80\x933 loss, England failed to qualify for the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2008" title="UEFA Euro 2008">Euro 2008 Finals</a>. Despite this, Beckham said that he has no plans to retire from international football and wanted to continue playing for the national team.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup> After being passed over by new England coach and Beckham\'s former manager at <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Capello" title="Fabio Capello">Fabio Capello</a>, for a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Switzerland_national_football_team" title="Switzerland national football team">Switzerland</a> which would have given him his hundredth cap; Beckham admitted that he was not in shape at the time, as he had not played a competitive match in three months.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span id="100_England_caps.2C_final_appearance"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="100_England_caps,_final_appearance">100 England caps, final appearance</span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham,_2008_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/David_Beckham%2C_2008_%28cropped%29.jpg/220px-David_Beckham%2C_2008_%28cropped%29.jpg" width="220" height="270" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/David_Beckham%2C_2008_%28cropped%29.jpg/330px-David_Beckham%2C_2008_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/David_Beckham%2C_2008_%28cropped%29.jpg/440px-David_Beckham%2C_2008_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1074" data-file-height="1317" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham,_2008_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham lining up a free kick for England in June 2008</div></div></div>\n<p>On 20 March 2008, Beckham was recalled to the England squad by Capello for the friendly against <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> in Paris on 26 March. Beckham became only the fifth Englishman to win 100 caps. Capello had hinted on 25 March 2008 that Beckham had a long-term future in his side ahead of crucial qualifiers for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>On 11 May 2008, Capello included an in-form Beckham in his 31-man England squad to face the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men&#39;s national soccer team">United States</a> at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a> on 28 May before the away fixture with <a href="/wiki/Trinidad_and_Tobago_national_football_team" title="Trinidad and Tobago national football team">Trinidad and Tobago</a> on 1 June. Beckham was honoured before the match by receiving an honorary gold cap representing his 100th cap from <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Charlton" title="Bobby Charlton">Bobby Charlton</a>, and was given a standing ovation from the crowd. He played well and assisted John Terry on the match-winning goal. When substituted at half-time for <a href="/wiki/David_Bentley" title="David Bentley">David Bentley</a>, the pro-Beckham crowd booed the decision.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup> In a surprise move, Capello handed Beckham the captaincy for England\'s friendly against Trinidad and Tobago on 1 June 2008. The match was the first time since the 2006 World Cup that Beckham had skippered England and marked a dramatic turnaround for Beckham. In two years, he had gone from being dropped completely from the England squad to being reinstated (though temporarily) as England captain.<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>During the 2010 World Cup Qualifier against <a href="/wiki/Belarus_national_football_team" title="Belarus national football team">Belarus</a> in which England won 3\xe2\x80\x931 in <a href="/wiki/Minsk" title="Minsk">Minsk</a>, Beckham came off the bench in the 87th minute to earn his 107th cap making him England\'s third-most-<a href="/wiki/Cap_(sport)" title="Cap (sport)">capped</a> player in history, overtaking Bobby Charlton in the process. On 11 February 2009, Beckham drew level with <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Moore" title="Bobby Moore">Bobby Moore</a>\'s record of 108 caps for an English outfield player, coming on as a substitute for <a href="/wiki/Stewart_Downing" title="Stewart Downing">Stewart Downing</a> in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> On 28 March 2009, Beckham surpassed Moore to hold the record outright when he came on as a substitute in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Slovakia_national_football_team" title="Slovakia national football team">Slovakia</a>, providing the assist for a goal from Wayne Rooney in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup> In all, Beckham had made 16 appearances out of a possible 20 for England under Capello until his ruptured Achilles tendon of March 2010 ruled him out of selection for the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> in South Africa.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture_192-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> His last game for England before injury had been on 14 October 2009 as a substitute in England\'s last World Cup qualifying game, which ended <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_6" title="2010 FIFA World Cup qualification \xe2\x80\x93 UEFA Group 6">England 3 \xe2\x80\x93 0 Belarus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture_192-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>After a poor performance from England at the World Cup, Capello remained as manager but was under pressure to revamp the England squad for the imminent <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2012_qualifying_Group_G" title="UEFA Euro 2012 qualifying Group G">UEFA Euro 2012 qualification campaign</a>. He unveiled a new team at the next England match, a home friendly game against Hungary on 11 August 2010, with Beckham still unavailable for selection but aiming for a return to playing in MLS by the following month.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture_192-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> In the post-match interview, Capello said of the prospect of the now 35-year-old Beckham playing any future competitive matches for England, that "I need to change it. David is a fantastic player but I think we need new players for the future", referring to the new players that play in Beckham\'s right midfield position, including <a href="/wiki/Theo_Walcott" title="Theo Walcott">Theo Walcott</a> and <a href="/wiki/Adam_Johnson_(footballer)" title="Adam Johnson (footballer)">Adam Johnson</a>, adding "This is the future of the team under Fabio Capello or another manager."<sup id="cite_ref-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture_192-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> He said that Beckham may be selected for one last friendly game, stating, "If he is fit, I hope we will play one more game here at Wembley so the fans can say goodbye." In response to the comments, Beckham\'s agent released a statement reiterating Beckham\'s position that he had no desire to retire from international football, and would always make himself available for selection for England if fit and if needed.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture_192-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> He remained 10 caps short of the record number of 125 caps by goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/Peter_Shilton" title="Peter Shilton">Peter Shilton</a>, for a player of any position.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture_192-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC11Aug2010NoEnglandFuture-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> Beckham was named in the provisional squad to represent the <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain_Olympic_football_team" title="Great Britain Olympic football team">Great Britain Olympic football team</a> at the 2012 Olympics.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> He was not included in the final selection by manager <a href="/wiki/Stuart_Pearce" title="Stuart Pearce">Stuart Pearce</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Approach_to_training_and_discipline">Approach to training and discipline</span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Training_and_praise_from_managers">Training and praise from managers</span></h3>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:28%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"David Beckham is Britain\'s finest striker of a football not because of God-given talent but because he practises with a relentless application that the vast majority of less gifted players wouldn\'t contemplate."</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94Former Manchester United manager <a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Alex Ferguson</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-guardian.co.uk_195-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-guardian.co.uk-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>Beckham was a product of Sir <a href="/wiki/Alex_Ferguson" title="Alex Ferguson">Alex Ferguson</a>\'s hard-working approach at Manchester United, and was renowned for his long-range passing, crossing ability, and <a href="/wiki/Curl_(football)" title="Curl (football)">bending</a> free-kicks as a right winger. Ferguson noted that Beckham "practised with a discipline to achieve an accuracy that other players wouldn\'t care about."<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> Beckham reportedly spent hours practising his free kicks after training sessions had ended.<sup id="cite_ref-guardian.co.uk_195-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-guardian.co.uk-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:25%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"What remains in your memory is his genuine commitment and dedication, his natural humility which he always had, that will stay forever."</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94Former Arsenal manager <a href="/wiki/Ars%C3%A8ne_Wenger" title="Ars\xc3\xa8ne Wenger">Ars\xc3\xa8ne Wenger</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Quote_199-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Quote-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>Beckham maintained his training routine at <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a> and even when his relationship with management was strained in early 2007, Real Madrid president <a href="/wiki/Ram%C3%B3n_Calder%C3%B3n" title="Ram\xc3\xb3n Calder\xc3\xb3n">Ram\xc3\xb3n Calder\xc3\xb3n</a> and manager <a href="/wiki/Fabio_Capello" title="Fabio Capello">Fabio Capello</a> praised Beckham for maintaining his professionalism and commitment to the club.<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> Beckham\'s Real Madrid teammate Roberto Carlos regarded Beckham to be the best free-kick exponent he had ever seen.<sup id="cite_ref-Roberto_Carlos_202-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roberto_Carlos-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup> Two of the best free kick exponents of their generation, <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Carlos" title="Roberto Carlos">Roberto Carlos</a> commented on the dilemma the team faced when they won a free kick on the edge of the penalty area: "I would stand on one side and Beckham on the other but I wanted to see Beckham take the free-kick because it\'s beautiful how he hits the ball."<sup id="cite_ref-Roberto_Carlos_202-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Roberto_Carlos-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In May 2013, asked about how he wanted to be remembered in his retirement, Beckham said, "I just want people to see me as a hardworking footballer, someone that\'s passionate about the game, someone that \xe2\x80\x93 every time I stepped on the pitch \xe2\x80\x93 I\'ve given everything that I have, because that\'s how I feel. That\'s how I look back on it and hope people will see me."<sup id="cite_ref-guardian.co.uk_195-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-guardian.co.uk-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Discipline">Discipline</span></h3>\n<p>Beckham was the first England player ever to collect two red cards, and the first England captain to be sent off.<sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> Beckham\'s most notorious red card was during the <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998 World Cup</a> after <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/Diego_Simeone" title="Diego Simeone">Diego Simeone</a> had fouled him: Beckham, lying face down on the pitch, kicked out at the Argentine midfielder, who fell dramatically.<sup id="cite_ref-Argentina_163-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Argentina-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>He amassed 41 yellow cards and four red cards in his time at Real Madrid; all four reds came in La Liga.<sup id="cite_ref-espnfc.com_204-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espnfc.com-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup> He received one red card while at Paris Saint-Germain, picked up in injury time in a match against <a href="/wiki/Evian_Thonon_Gaillard_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Evian Thonon Gaillard F.C.">Evian</a> on 28 April 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup> Between 2000 and 2013, Beckham played 420 competitive games for England, Milan, LA Galaxy, Manchester United, Real Madrid and PSG, and received seven red cards, one every 60 matches on average.<sup id="cite_ref-espnfc.com_204-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-espnfc.com-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="David_Beckham_Academy">David Beckham Academy</span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg/220px-David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg/330px-David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg/440px-David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3648" data-file-height="2736" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_Academy_London_at_night.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham Academy in London</div></div></div>\n<p>In 2005, Beckham founded the <a href="/wiki/David_Beckham_Academy" title="David Beckham Academy">David Beckham Academy</a> football school, operating from two sites, in London and Los Angeles. It was announced in late 2009 that both would close.<sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup> A mobile academy is being developed by Beckham, to travel around the UK and further afield.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_League_Soccer_team_in_Miami">Major League Soccer team in Miami</span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Inter_Miami_CF" title="Inter Miami CF">Inter Miami CF</a></div>\n<p>On 5 February 2014, MLS announced that Beckham had exercised his option to buy a <a href="/wiki/Expansion_of_Major_League_Soccer" title="Expansion of Major League Soccer">MLS expansion team</a> for $25&#160;million, which he had received as part of the contract he signed with the LA Galaxy in 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-Kennedy_96-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kennedy-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> The ownership group, led by Beckham, originally hoped the <a href="/wiki/Miami" title="Miami">Miami</a>-based team would begin play in 2016 or 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-Miami_Beckham_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Miami_Beckham-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> After delays getting a <a href="/wiki/Miami_MLS_stadium" title="Miami MLS stadium">stadium</a> deal completed, MLS announced in January 2018 that the team had been approved and would likely begin play in 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup> The team name and crest were revealed on 5 September. Club Internacional de Futbol Miami \xe2\x80\x93 more commonly known as, Inter Miami \xe2\x80\x93 is represented by a black crest with neon pink trimmings and herons whose legs clasp to form an "M" for Miami.<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg/170px-David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg" width="170" height="366" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg/255px-David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c5/David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg/340px-David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1716" data-file-height="3697" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_y_Victoria_Beckham.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham and his wife <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham" title="Victoria Beckham">Victoria</a> at the 2007 British Grand Prix at Silverstone</div></div></div>\n<p>In 1997, Beckham started dating <a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham" title="Victoria Beckham">Victoria Adams</a>, after she attended a Manchester United match.<sup id="cite_ref-mend_211-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mend-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-idolsw_213-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-idolsw-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> She was famously known as "Posh Spice" of the pop music group <a href="/wiki/Spice_Girls" title="Spice Girls">Spice Girls</a>, one of the world\'s top pop groups at the time, and his team was also enjoying a great run of success. Therefore, their relationship instantly attracted a great deal of media attention. The couple were dubbed "<a href="/wiki/Posh_and_Becks" title="Posh and Becks">Posh and Becks</a>" by the media.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> He proposed to her on 24 January 1998 in a restaurant in <a href="/wiki/Cheshunt" title="Cheshunt">Cheshunt</a>, England.\n</p><p>On 4 July 1999, they married at <a href="/wiki/Luttrellstown_Castle" title="Luttrellstown Castle">Luttrellstown Castle</a> in Ireland. Beckham\'s teammate <a href="/wiki/Gary_Neville" title="Gary Neville">Gary Neville</a> was the best man,<sup id="cite_ref-mend_211-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mend-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup> and the couple\'s infant son, Brooklyn, was the ring bearer.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup> The media were kept away from the ceremony, as the Beckhams had an exclusive deal with <i><a href="/wiki/OK!" title="OK!">OK! Magazine</a></i>, but newspapers were still able to obtain photographs showing them sitting on golden thrones.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup> 437 staff were employed for the wedding reception, which was estimated to have cost \xc2\xa3500,000.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>David and Victoria Beckham have four children: sons Brooklyn Joseph (born 4 March 1999 at Portland Hospital, London),<sup id="cite_ref-biography.com_218-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-biography.com-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup>  Romeo James (born 1 September 2002 at Portland Hospital, London),<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup> Cruz David (born 20 February 2005 at Ruber International Hospital,  Madrid),<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> and daughter Harper Seven (born 10 July 2011 at Cedars-Sinai Medical Center, Los Angeles).<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Elton_John" title="Elton John">Elton John</a> is godfather to Brooklyn and Romeo Beckham; their godmother is <a href="/wiki/Elizabeth_Hurley" title="Elizabeth Hurley">Elizabeth Hurley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup> Beckham\'s three sons have all played football in the <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C._Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Arsenal F.C. Academy">Arsenal Academy</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Brooklyn_223-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Brooklyn-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> Like their father, Brooklyn and Romeo have both done modelling work and been named among <a href="/wiki/GQ" title="GQ">GQ</a>\'s best dressed British men.<sup id="cite_ref-gq-magazine.co.uk_224-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gq-magazine.co.uk-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup> Brooklyn previously played football for <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C._Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Arsenal F.C. Academy">Arsenal U16</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Brooklyn_223-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Brooklyn-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup> but was released at the end of the 2014\xe2\x80\x9315 season.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In his early Manchester United career, Beckham lived in a four-bedroom house in <a href="/wiki/Worsley" title="Worsley">Worsley</a> that he bought directly from the property developer as a 20-year-old in 1995.<sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup> In 1999, shortly after his wedding he and Victoria bought a country house set in 24 acres in Sawbridgeworth, Hertfordshire, which the media nicknamed "<a href="/wiki/Beckingham_Palace" class="mw-redirect" title="Beckingham Palace">Beckingham Palace</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-beckingham_227-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-beckingham-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham suffers from <a href="/wiki/Obsessive_compulsive_disorder" class="mw-redirect" title="Obsessive compulsive disorder">obsessive compulsive disorder</a> (OCD), which he says makes him "have everything in a straight line or everything has to be in pairs." Victoria Beckham claims, "If you open our fridge, it\'s all co-ordinated down either side. We\'ve got three fridges \xe2\x80\x93 food in one, salad in another and drinks in the third. In the drinks one, everything is symmetrical. If there\'s three cans, he\'ll throw one away because it has to be an even number."<sup id="cite_ref-OCD_229-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OCD-229">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In April 2004, the British tabloid <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> carried claims by Beckham\'s former personal assistant <a href="/wiki/Rebecca_Loos" title="Rebecca Loos">Rebecca Loos</a> that he and Loos had an extramarital affair.<sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup> A week later, the Malaysian-born Australian model Sarah Marbeck claimed that she had slept with Beckham on two occasions. Beckham dismissed both accusations as "ludicrous".<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In September 2010, Beckham announced that he was making a court application against prostitute Irma Nici and several others over claims in the magazine <i>In Touch</i> that he had sex with her.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup> Although the magazine later accepted that the allegations against Beckham were untrue, his court application was dismissed under US freedom of speech laws.<sup id="cite_ref-234" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-234">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Outside_football">Outside football</span></h2>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_2009.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/David_Beckham_2009.jpg/170px-David_Beckham_2009.jpg" width="170" height="243" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/David_Beckham_2009.jpg/255px-David_Beckham_2009.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/David_Beckham_2009.jpg/340px-David_Beckham_2009.jpg 2x" data-file-width="644" data-file-height="922" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:David_Beckham_2009.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham in <a href="/wiki/Cape_Town" title="Cape Town">Cape Town</a>, South Africa, December 2009</div></div></div>\n<p>Beckham\'s fame extends beyond the <a href="/wiki/Association_football_pitch" class="mw-redirect" title="Association football pitch">pitch</a>; in much of the world his name is "as instantly recognisable as that of multinational companies like <a href="/wiki/Coca-Cola" title="Coca-Cola">Coca-Cola</a> and <a href="/wiki/IBM" title="IBM">IBM</a>."<sup id="cite_ref-thisismoney_236-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-thisismoney-236">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup> Beckham\'s relationship and marriage to Victoria, who has been famous in her own right as part of the <a href="/wiki/Spice_Girls" title="Spice Girls">Spice Girls</a>, contributed to his celebrity beyond football.\n</p><p>Beckham became known as a fashion icon, and together with Victoria, the couple became lucrative spokespeople sought after by clothing designers, health and fitness specialists, fashion magazines, perfume and cosmetics manufacturers, hair stylists, exercise promoters, and spa and recreation companies. One example is a line of aftershave and fragrances called David Beckham Instinct.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup> In 2002, Beckham was hailed as the ultimate "<a href="/wiki/Metrosexual" title="Metrosexual">metrosexual</a>" by the man who invented the term<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup> and has been described as such by numerous other articles since.<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The Beckhams were paid $13.7&#160;million in 2007 to launch his fragrance line in the United States<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup> In the world of fashion, David has already appeared on the covers of many magazines. United States covers have included the men\'s magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Details_(magazine)" title="Details (magazine)">Details</a></i>, and with his wife for the August 2007 issue of <i><a href="/wiki/W_(magazine)" title="W (magazine)">W</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup> According to Google, "David Beckham" was searched for more than any other sports topic on their site in 2003 and 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/Ask_Jeeves" class="mw-redirect" title="Ask Jeeves">Ask Jeeves</a>, Beckham ranked third, after <a href="/wiki/Britney_Spears" title="Britney Spears">Britney Spears</a> and <a href="/wiki/Osama_bin_Laden" title="Osama bin Laden">Osama bin Laden</a>, among subjects most searched for by British users of that site in the first decade of the 2000s.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg/220px-Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg" width="220" height="140" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg/330px-Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b8/Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg/440px-Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="508" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Michelle_Obama_with_David_Beckham_2013.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham with United States First Lady <a href="/wiki/Michelle_Obama" title="Michelle Obama">Michelle Obama</a> at the White House, March 2012</div></div></div>\n<p>Upon their arrival in Los Angeles on 12 July 2007, the night before Beckham\'s formal introduction, <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles_International_Airport" title="Los Angeles International Airport">Los Angeles International Airport</a> was filled with paparazzi and news reporters.<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup> On the next night, Victoria appeared on <i><a href="/wiki/The_Tonight_Show" title="The Tonight Show">The Tonight Show</a></i> with <a href="/wiki/Jay_Leno" title="Jay Leno">Jay Leno</a> to talk about their move to LA, and presented Leno with a number 23 Galaxy jersey with his own name on the back.
