Victoria also talked about her <a href="/wiki/NBC" title="NBC">NBC</a> TV show <i><a href="/wiki/Victoria_Beckham:_Coming_to_America" title="Victoria Beckham: Coming to America">Victoria Beckham: Coming to America</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">&#91;246&#93;</a></sup> On 22 July, a private welcoming party was held for the couple at the <a href="/wiki/Museum_of_Contemporary_Art,_Los_Angeles" title="Museum of Contemporary Art, Los Angeles">Museum of Contemporary Art, Los Angeles</a>. <a href="/wiki/A-list" title="A-list">A-list</a> celebrities attending included <a href="/wiki/Steven_Spielberg" title="Steven Spielberg">Steven Spielberg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jim_Carrey" title="Jim Carrey">Jim Carrey</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_Clooney" title="George Clooney">George Clooney</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tom_Cruise" title="Tom Cruise">Tom Cruise</a>, <a href="/wiki/Katie_Holmes" title="Katie Holmes">Katie Holmes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Will_Smith" title="Will Smith">Will Smith</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jada_Pinkett_Smith" title="Jada Pinkett Smith">Jada Pinkett Smith</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Oprah_Winfrey" title="Oprah Winfrey">Oprah Winfrey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">&#91;247&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham\'s many endorsement deals make him one of the most recognisable athletes throughout the world. Having worn <a href="/wiki/Adidas" title="Adidas">Adidas</a> football boots from the start of his career (notably <a href="/wiki/Adidas_Predator" title="Adidas Predator">Adidas Predator</a>), in 2003 he signed a $160&#160;million lifetime contract with Adidas, earning nearly half the money upfront, and will continue to earn percentages of profits on all of his branded Adidas products.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">&#91;248&#93;</a></sup> He had a 10-year collaboration with <a href="/wiki/Pepsi_Co." class="mw-redirect" title="Pepsi Co.">Pepsi Co.</a> that expired in 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">&#91;249&#93;</a></sup> He has also promoted <a href="/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company" title="The Walt Disney Company">The Walt Disney Company</a> theme parks.<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">&#91;250&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham has several eponymous video games, including <i><a href="/wiki/Go!_Go!_Beckham!_Adventure_on_Soccer_Island" title="Go! Go! Beckham! Adventure on Soccer Island">Go! Go! Beckham! Adventure on Soccer Island</a></i>, a <a href="/wiki/Platform_game" title="Platform game">platform game</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Game_Boy_Advance" title="Game Boy Advance">Game Boy Advance</a>, and <i><a href="/wiki/David_Beckham_Soccer" title="David Beckham Soccer">David Beckham Soccer</a></i>, a football game for a number of <a href="/wiki/Video_game_platforms#Platforms" class="mw-redirect" title="Video game platforms">platforms</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Eurogamer_251-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Eurogamer-251">&#91;251&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-beckhamxbox_252-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-beckhamxbox-252">&#91;252&#93;</a></sup> and he was brand ambassador for exercise video game <i><a href="/wiki/EA_Sports_Active_2" title="EA Sports Active 2">EA Sports Active 2</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">&#91;253&#93;</a></sup> Beckham featured in <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports</a>\' <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i> video game series</a>; he was on the cover for the International edition of <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA:_Road_to_World_Cup_98" title="FIFA: Road to World Cup 98">FIFA 98</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">&#91;254&#93;</a></sup> During his playing career (which ended in May 2013), Beckham generated an estimated \xc2\xa31 billion in <a href="/wiki/Kit_(association_football)#Basic_equipment" title="Kit (association football)">shirt</a> and <a href="/wiki/Football_boot" title="Football boot">boot</a> sales.<sup id="cite_ref-honours_255-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-honours-255">&#91;255&#93;</a></sup> In 2006, <a href="/wiki/Lloyd%27s_of_London" title="Lloyd&#39;s of London">Lloyd\'s of London</a> insured his legs for \xc2\xa3100m, at the time he was playing for Real Madrid.<sup id="cite_ref-256" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-256">&#91;256&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257">&#91;257&#93;</a></sup> In March 2015 Beckham had the third highest social media rank in the world among sportspeople, behind <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a>, with over 52 million Facebook fans.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">&#91;258&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg/220px-Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg/330px-Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg/440px-Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg 2x" data-file-width="5001" data-file-height="3334" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Vinfast-D.Beckham-Miss_Vietnam.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Beckham with Miss Vietnam at the Paris Motor Show 2018</div></div></div>\n<p>Beckham played a critical part in bringing the Olympics to London in 2012, travelling with the British delegation to <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a> in 2005 for the host city selection.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">&#91;259&#93;</a></sup> At the <a href="/wiki/2008_Beijing_Olympics" class="mw-redirect" title="2008 Beijing Olympics">2008 Beijing Olympics</a> closing ceremony, Beckham, <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Page" title="Jimmy Page">Jimmy Page</a> and <a href="/wiki/Leona_Lewis" title="Leona Lewis">Leona Lewis</a> represented Britain during the handover segment for the 2012 Olympics. Beckham rode a <a href="/wiki/AEC_Routemaster" title="AEC Routemaster">London double-decker bus</a> into the stadium and Page and Lewis performed "<a href="/wiki/Whole_Lotta_Love" title="Whole Lotta Love">Whole Lotta Love</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup> He also featured at the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics_opening_ceremony" title="2012 Summer Olympics opening ceremony">Opening Ceremony</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2012_Summer_Olympics" title="2012 Summer Olympics">2012 London Olympics</a>, carrying the <a href="/wiki/Olympic_flame" title="Olympic flame">Olympic flame</a> to the <a href="/wiki/London_Stadium" title="London Stadium">stadium</a> by speedboat.<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">&#91;261&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham visited <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> in May 2010 for a morale-boosting visit to British troops fighting the <a href="/wiki/Taliban_insurgency" title="Taliban insurgency">Taliban insurgency</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262">&#91;262&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-263" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-263">&#91;263&#93;</a></sup> The appearance of Beckham as well as British Foreign Secretary <a href="/wiki/William_Hague" title="William Hague">William Hague</a> and Defence Secretary <a href="/wiki/Liam_Fox" title="Liam Fox">Liam Fox</a> was believed to have prompted a <a href="/wiki/Taliban" title="Taliban">Taliban</a> attack on <a href="/wiki/Kandahar" title="Kandahar">Kandahar</a> airfield.<sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">&#91;264&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">&#91;265&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Chinese authorities appointed Beckham as global ambassador for Chinese football in March 2013. After numerous officials had been banned for match-fixing, and the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Super_League" title="Chinese Super League">Chinese Super League</a> had failed to retain the services of well-known international names, Beckham\'s role was to help improve the image of the game and raise its profile both in China and abroad.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">&#91;266&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>From 14 July 2013, Beckham started appearing in adverts for <a href="/wiki/BSkyB" class="mw-redirect" title="BSkyB">BSkyB</a> advertising their <a href="/wiki/Sky_Sports" title="Sky Sports">Sky Sports</a> coverage via the <a href="/wiki/Sky_Go" title="Sky Go">Sky Go</a> app.<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">&#91;267&#93;</a></sup> In January 2014, Beckham appeared on <i><a href="/wiki/Late_Night_with_Jimmy_Fallon" title="Late Night with Jimmy Fallon">Late Night with Jimmy Fallon</a></i> on NBC in the U.S, and in March he made a guest appearance in the BBC\'s <a href="/wiki/Sport_Relief_2014_Special" title="Sport Relief 2014 Special">Sport Relief special</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Only_Fools_and_Horses" title="Only Fools and Horses">Only Fools and Horses</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268">&#91;268&#93;</a></sup> He was named one of <i><a href="/wiki/GQ" title="GQ">GQ</a></i><span class="nowrap" style="padding-left:0.1em;">&#39;</span>s 50 best dressed British men in 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-gq-magazine.co.uk_224-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gq-magazine.co.uk-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham was announced as the new Ambassadorial president of the <a href="/wiki/British_Fashion_Council" title="British Fashion Council">British Fashion Council</a> on 11 May 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269">&#91;269&#93;</a></sup> Prior to the June 2018 vote by FIFA member nations for selecting the hosts of the <a href="/wiki/2026_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2026 FIFA World Cup">2026 FIFA World Cup</a>, Beckham endorsed the <a href="/wiki/United_2026_FIFA_World_Cup_bid" title="United 2026 FIFA World Cup bid">North American bid</a> (Canada, Mexico and the United States).<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270">&#91;270&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Charitable_work">Charitable work</span></h2>\n<p>Beckham has supported <a href="/wiki/UNICEF" title="UNICEF">UNICEF</a> since his days at <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> and in January 2005, the English national team captain became a Goodwill Ambassador with a special focus on UNICEF\'s Sports for Development program.<sup id="cite_ref-UNICEF_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNICEF-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> In 2012, he met with UK Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> at <a href="/wiki/10_Downing_Street" title="10 Downing Street">10 Downing Street</a> to call for more action to help children affected by <a href="/wiki/Malnutrition" title="Malnutrition">malnutrition</a> around the world.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">&#91;271&#93;</a></sup> In 2015, his tenth year as a UNICEF Ambassador, Beckham launched <i>7: The David Beckham UNICEF Fund</i> to help protect children in danger.<sup id="cite_ref-UNICEF_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNICEF-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> In June 2015 he visited <a href="/wiki/Siem_Reap" title="Siem Reap">Siem Reap</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a>, where he met with child victims of violence.<sup id="cite_ref-UNICEF_20-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNICEF-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Beckham has pledged his support for the <a href="/wiki/Unite_for_Children,_Unite_Against_AIDS" title="Unite for Children, Unite Against AIDS">Unite for Children, Unite Against AIDS</a> campaign. He is a former patron of the <a href="/wiki/Elton_John_AIDS_Foundation" title="Elton John AIDS Foundation">Elton John AIDS Foundation</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">&#91;272&#93;</a></sup> In 2013, he also donated all his \xc2\xa33.4 million salary taken from <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain" class="mw-redirect" title="Paris Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</a> to two children\'s charities in France.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">&#91;273&#93;</a></sup> Beckham has been supporting the charity named <a href="/wiki/Help_For_Heroes" class="mw-redirect" title="Help For Heroes">Help For Heroes</a> for many years whose aim is to help soldiers injured in Iraq and Afghan wars.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">&#91;274&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>On 17 January 2007, Rebecca Johnstone, a 19-year-old cancer patient from <a href="/wiki/Hamilton,_Ontario" title="Hamilton, Ontario">Hamilton, Ontario</a>, Canada, received a surprise phone call from Beckham. After the conversation, he sent her a Real Madrid jersey with his signature on it. Rebecca died on 29 January 2007.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">&#91;275&#93;</a></sup> On 1 July 2007, Beckham appeared as a speaker at the <a href="/wiki/Concert_for_Diana" title="Concert for Diana">Concert for Diana</a> held at <a href="/wiki/Wembley_Stadium" title="Wembley Stadium">Wembley Stadium</a>, London to celebrate the life of <a href="/wiki/Diana,_Princess_of_Wales" title="Diana, Princess of Wales">Princess Diana</a> almost 10 years after her death.<sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276">&#91;276&#93;</a></sup> Proceeds from the concert went to Diana\'s charities as well as to charities of which her sons Princes William and Harry are patrons.<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277">&#91;277&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-278" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-278">&#91;278&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham is a founding member of the <a href="/wiki/Malaria_No_More_UK" title="Malaria No More UK">Malaria No More UK</a> Leadership Council and helped launch the charity in 2009 with <a href="/wiki/Andy_Murray" title="Andy Murray">Andy Murray</a> at Wembley Stadium. Beckham also appeared in a 2007 public service announcement for <a href="/wiki/Malaria_No_More" title="Malaria No More">Malaria No More</a> U.S, advertising the need for inexpensive bed nets. The TV spot aired in the United States on <a href="/wiki/Fox_Broadcasting_Company" title="Fox Broadcasting Company">Fox Networks</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Fox_Soccer_Channel" class="mw-redirect" title="Fox Soccer Channel">Fox Soccer Channel</a>, and can also be seen on YouTube.<sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279">&#91;279&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Since joining <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a>, Beckham has been a very public advocate in the United States for related charities such as "MLS W.O.R.K.S." On 17 August 2007, he conducted a youth clinic in <a href="/wiki/Harlem" title="Harlem">Harlem</a>, along with other current and former MLS players. This was in advance of his first New York City area match the following day against the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Red_Bulls" title="New York Red Bulls">New York Red Bulls</a>. That team\'s <a href="/wiki/Jozy_Altidore" title="Jozy Altidore">Jozy Altidore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Juan_Pablo_%C3%81ngel" title="Juan Pablo \xc3\x81ngel">Juan Pablo \xc3\x81ngel</a> were also with Beckham, teaching skills to disadvantaged youth to benefit <a href="/wiki/Harlem_Youth_Soccer_Association" title="Harlem Youth Soccer Association">FC Harlem Lions</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-280" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-280">&#91;280&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearances_in_films">Appearances in films</span></h2>\n<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:27%;&#32;;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r856303512"/>\n<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"We may be a small country, but we\'re a great one, too. The country of Shakespeare, Churchill, the Beatles, Sean Connery, Harry Potter. David Beckham\'s right foot. David Beckham\'s left foot, come to that."</div>\n<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">\xe2\x80\x94<a href="/wiki/Hugh_Grant" title="Hugh Grant">Hugh Grant</a>\xe2\x80\x99s character in the 2003 film  <i><a href="/wiki/Love_Actually" title="Love Actually">Love Actually</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-Quote_199-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Quote-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup></cite>\n</p>\n</div>\n<p>Beckham never personally appeared in the 2002 film <i><a href="/wiki/Bend_It_Like_Beckham" title="Bend It Like Beckham">Bend It Like Beckham</a></i>, except in archive footage. He and his wife wanted to make cameo appearances, but scheduling proved difficult, so the director used lookalike <a href="/wiki/Andy_Harmer" title="Andy Harmer">Andy Harmer</a> instead.<sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281">&#91;281&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham makes a cameo appearance with Zinedine Zidane and Ra\xc3\xbal, in the 2005 film <i><a href="/wiki/Goal!_(film)" title="Goal! (film)">Goal!</a></i>. Harmer also doubled for him in the party scene.<sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282">&#91;282&#93;</a></sup> Beckham himself appears in the sequel <i><a href="/wiki/Goal_II:_Living_the_Dream" title="Goal II: Living the Dream">Goal II: Living the Dream</a></i><sup id="cite_ref-283" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-283">&#91;283&#93;</a></sup> in a larger role, when the film\'s lead character gets transferred to Real Madrid. This time, the story centres on the Real Madrid team, and besides Beckham, other real life Real Madrid players also appear on and off the pitch, alongside the fictional characters. Though the use of stock footage from the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 FIFA World Cup</a>, Beckham appeared in <i><a href="/wiki/Goal_III:_Taking_on_the_World" title="Goal III: Taking on the World">Goal III: Taking on the World</a></i>, which was released <a href="/wiki/Direct-to-video" title="Direct-to-video">straight to DVD</a> on 15 June 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284">&#91;284&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham has expressed no interest in pursuit of acting roles, saying he is too "stiff".<sup id="cite_ref-285" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-285">&#91;285&#93;</a></sup> However, due to his friendship with <a href="/wiki/Guy_Ritchie" title="Guy Ritchie">Guy Ritchie</a>, he has made two cameo appearances in Ritchie\'s films: as a projectionist in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Man_from_U.N.C.L.E._(film)" title="The Man from U.N.C.L.E. (film)">The Man from U.N.C.L.E.</a></i> (based on the 1964 <a href="/wiki/Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer" title="Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer">MGM</a> <a href="/wiki/The_Man_from_U.N.C.L.E." title="The Man from U.N.C.L.E.">television series of the same name</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286">&#91;286&#93;</a></sup> and as Trigger in <i><a href="/wiki/King_Arthur:_Legend_of_the_Sword" title="King Arthur: Legend of the Sword">King Arthur: Legend of the Sword</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287">&#91;287&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Beckham has played along to jokes about his voice. In a 2018 promo for <i><a href="/wiki/Deadpool_2" title="Deadpool 2">Deadpool 2</a></i>, Beckham is seen watching the <a href="/wiki/Deadpool_(film)" title="Deadpool (film)">first instalment of the film franchise</a> in which <a href="/wiki/Ryan_Reynolds" title="Ryan Reynolds">Ryan Reynolds</a>\' character compares Beckham\'s voice to inhaling helium.<sup id="cite_ref-Deadpool_288-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Deadpool-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup> Beckham is seen rolling his eyes at the voice jibe before receiving an apology text from Deadpool. Beckham answers his door to the antihero who presents him with milk and cookies, before Deadpool knocks again and has a bunch of helium-filled red balloons.<sup id="cite_ref-Deadpool_288-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Deadpool-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Records">Records</span></h2>\n<p>Beckham captained <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> 59 times,<sup id="cite_ref-289" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-289">&#91;289&#93;</a></sup> the fourth highest after <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Moore" title="Bobby Moore">Bobby Moore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Billy_Wright_(footballer_born_1924)" class="mw-redirect" title="Billy Wright (footballer born 1924)">Billy Wright</a> both with 90, and <a href="/wiki/Bryan_Robson" title="Bryan Robson">Bryan Robson</a> with 65. With his free kick goal against <a href="/wiki/Ecuador_national_football_team" title="Ecuador national football team">Ecuador</a> in the second round of the <a href="/wiki/2006_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2006 FIFA World Cup">2006 World Cup</a>, Beckham gained membership into two of football\'s exclusive clubs: he became the only English player \xe2\x80\x93 and the 21st player in the world \xe2\x80\x93 to score in three World Cups; Real Madrid teammate <a href="/wiki/Ra%C3%BAl_(footballer)" title="Ra\xc3\xbal (footballer)">Ra\xc3\xbal</a> also achieved this feat a few days earlier.<sup id="cite_ref-290" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-290">&#91;290&#93;</a></sup> It also made him only the fifth player in World Cup history to score twice from a direct free kick; the other four were <a href="/wiki/Pel%C3%A9" title="Pel\xc3\xa9">Pel\xc3\xa9</a>, <a href="/wiki/Roberto_Rivelino" class="mw-redirect" title="Roberto Rivelino">Roberto Rivelino</a>, <a href="/wiki/Te%C3%B3filo_Cubillas" title="Te\xc3\xb3filo Cubillas">Te\xc3\xb3filo Cubillas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Bernard_Genghini" title="Bernard Genghini">Bernard Genghini</a> (Beckham had previously scored this way against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> in the first round of the <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998 World Cup</a>). All three goals were against South American teams (Colombia, <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a> and Ecuador) and from set pieces (the two aforementioned free kicks and a penalty against Argentina).<sup id="cite_ref-Colombia_162-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Colombia-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Ecuador_177-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ecuador-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tattoos">Tattoos</span></h2>\n<p>As of 2017, Beckham had more than 50 tattoos.<sup id="cite_ref-291" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-291">&#91;291&#93;</a></sup> There are names of his sons Romeo, Cruz and Brooklyn, and of his wife Victoria. His wife\'s name, tattooed on his left forearm, is in <a href="/wiki/Sanskrit" title="Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a> script because Beckham thought it would be "tacky" to have it in English. However, this was misspelt as the equivalent of "Vihctoria".<sup id="cite_ref-292" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-292">&#91;292&#93;</a></sup> In his autobiography <i>David Beckham: My Side</i>, he said that the idea of having tattoos came to him in 1999 after his son Brooklyn was born, following a conversation on the subject of tattoos with <a href="/wiki/Melanie_Brown" class="mw-redirect" title="Melanie Brown">Mel B</a> and her then-husband, Jimmy Gulzar. Beckham said: "When you see me, you see the tattoos. You see an expression of how I feel about Victoria and the boys. They\'re part of me."<sup id="cite_ref-293" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-293">&#91;293&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, Beckham added to his collection with a tattoo of a solar system covering the left side of his scalp.<sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294">&#91;294&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Awards">Awards</span></h2>\n<table id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296">&#91;296&#93;</a></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career
